:   "*I want only to bring peace and order to the galaxy.*"  
    "*Already so many have suffered for what you call 'order'.*"  
    "*Then let me give you peace, Master Yaddle.*"
:   ―Dooku and Yaddle — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/DookuKillsYaddle.flac/revision/latest?cb=20251119143258)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:DookuKillsYaddle.flac "File:DookuKillsYaddle.flac"))[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

**Dooku** was a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [Serennian](/wiki/Serennian "Serennian") who served as a [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") during the [waning years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and later [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") of [House Serenno](/wiki/House_Serenno "House Serenno"). He became dissatisfied with the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and fell to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), becoming the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") **Darth Tyranus**. After [leaving](/wiki/Lost_Twenty "Lost Twenty") the Jedi Order, he served as [Count](/wiki/House_Serenno "House Serenno") of [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno") and [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State") of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). He was the second [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") of [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), the Dark Lord of the Sith, whose plan to conquer [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") relied on Dooku leading a pan-[galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") [secessionist movement](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") against the Republic. As such, Dooku immersed himself in the dark side of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") and worked tirelessly to advance his and his [master's](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") [Grand Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") while being unaware that he was merely a pawn of his master.

[Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY") during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), Dooku was taken by the Jedi Order after being abandoned by his [family](/wiki/House_Serenno "House Serenno") and [learned](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") the Jedi arts as the [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") of [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), the legendary [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") of the Jedi Order; he went on to take the maverick [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") as his own apprentice. A [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") idealist, the corruption in the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate")—as well as the [traditions of the Jedi](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code")—disillusioned him. In [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY") Dooku left the Order and returned to his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"), where he reclaimed his title of Count and heritage as a [nobleman](/wiki/Noble "Noble") after [overthrowing](/wiki/Incident_on_Serenno "Incident on Serenno") his corrupt brother, [Ramil](/wiki/Ramil "Ramil"). His former peers believed his decision was misguided but still held him in high esteem. However the Count of Serenno began to secretly conspire with Darth Sidious. After the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of Qui-Gon Jinn at the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"), and following the [duel](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Works "Duel in the Works") in [the Works](/wiki/The_Works "The Works") which saw the death of Jedi Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle"), Dooku embraced the dark side and adopted the name of Darth Tyranus upon fully becoming the apprentice of Darth Sidious. Throughout the first [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") of Sheev Palpatine's [chancellery](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"), Dooku used his resources and charisma to recruit entire [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") to the Separatist cause. At the same [time](/wiki/Time "Time"), he oversaw the development of two vast [armies](/wiki/Army "Army") that would be pitted against each other in the conflict to come: the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), which consisted of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") manufactured on worlds such as [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"); and the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"), composed of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") [bred](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") on [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") and [modeled](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") on the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett").

After [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of maneuvering the galaxy into a state of war, the Clone Wars began when the newly formed [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") [invaded Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). As leader of the Separatists, Dooku delegated [military](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military") authority to a cadre of subordinates personally trained by himself, including [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") and [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"). While Grievous was trained only in the art of [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat"), Ventress was [strong](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") with [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), affording her the opportunity to learn the ways of the dark side from Dooku. The Sith, however, remained faithful to [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane")'s [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"); and as such, Dooku was compelled to betray his disciple after Sidious became suspicious of his own apprentice's intentions. Though he sought to replace Ventress with [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress") and later [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"), Dooku ultimately remained beholden to his master's will, which would eventually be his undoing.

By the third year of the war, Dooku and Grievous succeeded in abducting Chancellor Palpatine (per Sidious' plan) from the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). During the ensuing [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), he was [confronted](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") and defeated by the [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), who summarily [executed](/wiki/Death_penalty "Death penalty") the Count via [beheading](/wiki/Death "Death") at the Chancellor's behest. In the [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") following Dooku's death, Palpatine revealed to the Jedi that he was, in fact, Darth Sidious, who betrayed his apprentice in order to replace him with the younger and more promising Skywalker. With the subsequent [fall of the Jedi Order](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), Sidious [consolidated his power](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") upon [declaring](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), which Tyranus had an instrumental role in establishing. As for Skywalker, he succeeded the late Darth Tyranus as Sidious' third and last apprentice, resulting in his transformation into Darth Vader and proving his slain victim's words of sensing fear, hate, and anger.

## Biography[]

### Early life[]

#### Jedi induction and initiation[]

Dooku was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY") during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno") to the planet's ruler, [Count](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno "Count of Serenno") [Gora](/wiki/Gora "Gora"), and his [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), [Countess](/wiki/Countess "Countess") [Anya](/wiki/Anya_(Serenno) "Anya (Serenno)"). The [child's](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") [Force-sensitivity](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") manifested itself rapidly, scaring his [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), who hated and feared those he dismissed as "freaks." Gora contacted the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and told them to take his son. However, instead of waiting for the [Jedi seekers](/wiki/Jedi_seeker "Jedi seeker") to arrive, Gora abandoned the infant outside his palace on the edges of the forest without [clothes](/wiki/Clothing "Clothing") or any form of identification. A seeker rescued Dooku before he froze to [death](/wiki/Death "Death") or was eaten by [spine-wolves](/wiki/Spine-wolves "Spine-wolves"), and brought the child to the [Jedi Grand Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

#### Life as a youngling[]

 [![Dooku was raised in the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, where he learned the ways of the Force alongside other younglings.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Temple_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest?cb=20200403145030) [![Dooku was raised in the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, where he learned the ways of the Force alongside other younglings.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Temple_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403145030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Temple_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest?cb=20200403145030) 

Dooku was raised in the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, where he learned the ways of the Force alongside other younglings.

 

Dooku was integrated into [Hawk-Bat Clan](/wiki/Hawk-Bat_Clan "Hawk-Bat Clan") alongside fellow younglings [Zang Arraira](/wiki/Zang_Arraira "Zang Arraira"), [Arath Tarrex](/wiki/Arath_Tarrex "Arath Tarrex"), and [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), under the direction of the [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Tera Sinube](/wiki/Tera_Sinube "Tera Sinube"). During his [time](/wiki/Time "Time") as a [Jedi youngling](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate"), he continuously strove to excel, working himself hard to achieve better results than his peers and always striving to remain within the boundaries of the rules set by his teachers. Dooku therefore distanced himself from the other younglings rather than try to befriend them. His talents made him clash with fellow youngling Tarrex, largely due to the latter's jealousy over Dooku's superior abilities. Tarrex frequently insulted Dooku, calling him 'His Excellency' due to his imperious and somewhat aristocratic manner. Dooku and Sifo-Dyas were close friends during their time as younglings, and on one occasion[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) in [90 BBY](/wiki/90_BBY "90 BBY")[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) accompanied [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") Yoda and Masters Sinube and [Yula Braylon](/wiki/Yula_Braylon "Yula Braylon") to Serenno for the [galactic festival](/wiki/Celebration_on_Serenno "Celebration on Serenno") being held there with other Jedi in tow.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

As the Masters were demonstrating the proper lightsaber stances, a pair of children set off some thunderburst caps and ran off, Dooku thought he recognized one of them and followed them out to the fairgrounds. There he found the two being harassed by a trio of thugs that were threatening to kidnap them, Dooku used his Force powers and an electroblade to force the criminals to back off. Afterwards, the pair introduced themselves as [Jenza](/wiki/Jenza "Jenza") and [Ramil](/wiki/Ramil "Ramil"), though the latter was less than thankful for the Jedi's assistance. When she learned Dooku was from Serenno, Jenza offered to give Dooku a tour of the homeworld he never knew.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

They explored the celebration together playing games and tasting the food, becoming fast friends as they got to know each other. Eventually, Jenza took Dooku to the [Great Assembly](/wiki/Great_Assembly_House "Great Assembly House"), where she showed him the seals of the seven houses and told him the legend of how her ancestors liberated the planet from the Sith Empire. Though before they could leave Dooku felt drawn to an ancient carving of a beast, that was identified by Jenza as a [Tirra'Taka](/wiki/Tirra%27Taka "Tirra'Taka"). Ignoring her warning that it was bad luck, he moved to touch it, and as his finger brushed the stone, a [groundquake](/wiki/Groundquake "Groundquake") caused the building around them to collapse.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Though Dooku attempted to lift the debris off of them himself, it took the intervention of Master Yoda to free the the two from the rubble. Once the other Masters helped the Grand Master remove the collapsed structure from the area, Count Gora of Serenno furiously confronted Yoda when he heard Dooku's name being voiced, yelling at the Jedi that he never wished to see his son again. It was here that the young Jedi learned that Gora was his Father and Jenza his sister.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Shocked and confused by his father's behavior, Dooku later questioned Yoda about how he was brought into the Jedi Order. The elder Jedi revealed that Gora had contacted the Jedi upon discovering his son's Force-sensitivity, and that he had left Dooku outside his castle walls without clothes or identification. Dooku would learn shortly after that being left on the edge of the forest put him at risk of being eaten alive by Spine-wolves had he not been found. Upon arriving back at the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, his injuries were quickly healed and the young Jedi quickly threw himself back into his training. Dooku using this practice to vent his frustrations at Count Gora for abandoning him, and furthermore to think deeply about what he might have been if he had never become a Jedi. At this time an attendant arrived with a communications device that would allow him to speak to his sister, and they stayed in contact for many years.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

[Two years later](/wiki/88_BBY "88 BBY"), after a lesson in the Jedi Archives Sifo-Dyas revealed to Dooku he had come into possession of the journal of the expelled Jedi; [Klias Teradine](/wiki/Klias_Teradine "Klias Teradine"), which revealed to him the existence of the [Bogan Collection](/wiki/Archive_of_Forbidden_Artifacts "Archive of Forbidden Artifacts") inside the Jedi Archives. Sifo convinced Dooku that they should break in to see the dark side artifacts. Dooku later used sand levitation to get past the magnetic lock. There they witnessed many dark objects, weapons, and scrolls the Jedi had collected over their history. Dooku in particular was drawn to a piece of metal that seemed to connect him to the same Tirra'Taka he had first encountered on Serenno. This frightened the boy, who lashed out through the Force and accidentally threw Sifo-Dyas through a cabinet, alerting the Chief Librarian, [Restelly Quist](/wiki/Restelly_Quist "Restelly Quist"), to their actions.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

The two initiates were brought to the infirmary where Sifo's injuries were treated, and they were confronted by Masters Yoda and Braylon, who each expressed a deep disappointment in how they had broken the rules and betrayed their trust. As the Masters were lecturing them, their discussion was interrupted by the arrival of [Lene Kostana](/wiki/Lene_Kostana "Lene Kostana"), who expressed great concern over the security of the [Bogan Collection](/wiki/Bogan_Collection "Bogan Collection") since two younglings had been able to break in. Dooku and Sifo-Dyas watched the Masters debate their conflicting views on how best to train the next generation to confront the Dark Side. Afterwards, they were assigned to decipher the [Lothal Papyri](/wiki/Lothal_Papyri "Lothal Papyri"), a collection of agricultural treatises, under the watchful eyes of Librarian Quist. As they served their penance, they had another encounter with Lene Kostana who was surprised that Yoda was still using the same treatises as punishment for misbehaved younglings, and playfully referred to the Grand Master as a goblin which offended Dooku. As she left, Sifo-Dyas discovered she slipped him a book: *[The Bestiary of Darth Caldoth](/wiki/The_Bestiary_of_Darth_Caldoth "The Bestiary of Darth Caldoth")*. Dooku encouraged his friend to tell someone about the text, but Sifo refused.

This event greatly disturbed Dooku, who began to think Master Kostana might secretly be a Sith, one day he confronted her on the [contemplation balcony](/wiki/Contemplation_balcony "Contemplation balcony") demanding to know why she gave his friend the Sith script. She said the book was a test, though Dooku sensed a great deal of frustration and anger in her which he believed legitimized his theory. The two engaged in a short duel, during which Master Kostana played an act of goading him on, using the tale of [Darth Sakia](/wiki/Darth_Sakia "Darth Sakia") as a lesson by comparing Dooku's [curved-hilt lightsaber](/wiki/Curved-hilt_lightsaber "Curved-hilt lightsaber") to the fictional Sith's weapon, and revealing she was aware of Dooku's curious connection to the Tirra'Taka. Unfortunately Kostana quickly lost control of the situation as Dooku began a frenzy of attacks that began wearing down her defenses. Their fight was broken up by the timely intervention of Master Yoda who calmed the initiate down and convinced him that he had jumped to conclusions. The Grand Master then chided the Altiri on her constant need to test the initiates by exposing them to dark side artifacts. Following this event Dooku began to spend more time with Master Kostana, as he started to look to her as a mentor figure, since he took a great deal of interest in her work studying the dark side, her theories concerning the Sith, and even her pet [Convor](/wiki/Convor "Convor") Ferana. He visited her nearly every time she returned to the Temple following her missions.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

#### The Grand Master's apprentice[]

:   "*Perhaps the best Padawan of your generation, you were.*"  
    "*Are you resorting to* flattery*, Master Yoda? Besides, I recall getting into more* trouble *than any other Padawan of my generation.*"  
    "*Yes. And a* valuable *perspective, this gives you.*"
:   ―Yoda and Dooku reflect on their time together as master and apprentice[[22]](#cite_note-Yoda_4-22)

 [![Dooku was the Padawan of Grand Master Yoda and grew into an esteemed Jedi in his own right.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Dookugrowsup-Yoda4.png/revision/latest?cb=20251103194625) [![Dooku was the Padawan of Grand Master Yoda and grew into an esteemed Jedi in his own right.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Dookugrowsup-Yoda4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20251103194625)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Dookugrowsup-Yoda4.png/revision/latest?cb=20251103194625) 

Dooku was the Padawan of Grand Master Yoda and grew into an esteemed Jedi in his own right.

 

In [86 BBY](/wiki/86_BBY "86 BBY"),[[23]](#cite_note-86_BBY-23) Dooku later completed his [Initiate Trials](/wiki/Initiate_Trials "Initiate Trials") and hoped to be selected as the Padawan apprentice to Lene Kostana due to her mission in hunting down relics associated with the dark side. During the Padawan Tournament, Dooku fought and defeated Sifo-Dyas in a duel with one hand behind his back and blindfolded. However, Kostana selected Sifo-Dyas as her apprentice, which upset Dooku, though this disappointment subsided when he learned that Yoda had decided to take him as his apprentice.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

A strong bond developed between Dooku and Yoda as his training continued.[[24]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-24) On one occasion, Yoda took Dooku on a voyage to [Lahsbane](/wiki/Lahsbane "Lahsbane") in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") as part of his training.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) During a mission to [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), Dooku watched as his master faced a giant [Terentatek](/wiki/Terentatek "Terentatek").[[9]](#cite_note-Destiny-9)

#### Sifo-Dyas' vision[]

Sometime around [85 BBY](/wiki/85_BBY "85 BBY"),[[25]](#cite_note-85_BBY_date-25) Sifo-Dyas received a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") of a deadly solar storm hitting the planet [Protobranch](/wiki/Protobranch "Protobranch"). After informing the Jedi Council, Dooku supported Sifo-Dyas and Kostana's suggestion that they warn the planet, but was forbidden to by Yoda and the Council, who pointed out that Force visions were not absolute and the future was always in motion.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Frustrated with the Council, Dooku, Kostana, and Sifo-Dyas went behind the Council's back to inform [Tavetti](/wiki/Tavetti "Tavetti"), the senator who represented Protobranch, of the vision. During the conversation, Dooku was slightly unnerved by Tavetti only expressing concern for Protobranch's resources rather than its people. Afterwards, Dooku, Kostana, Sifo-Dyas and a reluctant Yoda went to the planet itself. Ultimately, Sifo-Dyas' vision came to pass; a [powerful solar storm](/wiki/Protobranch_solar_storm "Protobranch solar storm") hit Protobranch, killing much of the population, with the Jedi themselves barely surviving.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

The events with Protobranch shook Dooku's respect for the Republic and the Jedi Council, feeling the latter was somewhat responsible for the deaths that occurred by not taking Sifo-Dyas' vision seriously and refusing to act quicker. He was also disgusted by the fact that the Republic's primary concern was the loss of Protobranch's resources and not its inhabitants.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

#### Funeral of Anya[]

Around [82 BBY](/wiki/82_BBY "82 BBY"),[[26]](#cite_note-82_BBY-26) a twenty year old Dooku attended the funeral of his mother, Anya, on Serenno. It was here that his father Gora physically and verbally assaulted him, referring to his son as a "freak." Shortly afterward, Dooku joined Sifo-Dyas and his master Kostana on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Asusto "Mission to Asusto") to track down a relic on [Asusto](/wiki/Asusto "Asusto"). However, the pair were led into a trap by the [Presagers of Hakotei](/wiki/Presagers_of_Hakotei "Presagers of Hakotei") who tricked them into following a supposed trail of [Sith artifacts](/wiki/Sith_artifact "Sith artifact") from [Karazak](/wiki/Karazak "Karazak"). Dooku was briefly captured by the Presagers to be used as part of a dark side ritual. It was during his brief captivity that he experienced a series of visions of his future, and he used [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") for the first time in order to kill his captors. After which Master Kostana and Sifo-Dyas taught him a cleansing ritual involving arm wrappings that was designed to keep him centered in the force.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

### Jedi Master[]

#### Attaining the rank[]

:   "*You know, My Lady, Count Dooku was once a Jedi. He couldn't assassinate anyone. It's not in his character.*"
:   ―Jedi Master Mace Windu, to [Senator Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala")[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

Between [82 BBY](/wiki/82_BBY "82 BBY") and [78 BBY](/wiki/78_BBY "78 BBY"), Dooku completed his training with Yoda and became a Jedi Knight and eventually Jedi Master, rising to be one of the greatest Jedi of his generation. A veteran of many galactic conflicts, he was known for his exceptional skills as a lightsaber duelist.[[27]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars,_New_Edition-27) He would take [Rael Averross](/wiki/Rael_Averross "Rael Averross") as his Padawan, training him for 10 years and to Knighthood. Dooku had also set aside his [first blade](/wiki/Dooku%27s_first_lightsaber "Dooku's first lightsaber") and created [his own curved-hilt lightsaber](/wiki/Dooku%27s_lightsaber "Dooku's lightsaber"),[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28) which produced a blue blade. Dooku used his lightsaber when he and Yoda demonstrated their lightsaber skills to a group of younglings, amongst them the [Togorian](/wiki/Togorian "Togorian") [Jak'zin](/wiki/Jak%27zin "Jak'zin").[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29) Furthermore, Dooku was the main lightsaber instructor for [Thranta Clan](/wiki/Thranta_Clan "Thranta Clan").[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Dooku also rendered aid to [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Talzin](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin") of the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters"), who were based on the world of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"),[[30]](#cite_note-Monster-30) giving her a lock of his hair.[[8]](#cite_note-Massacre-8)

#### Training Qui-Gon[]

:   "*Qui-Gon Jinn would never join you.*"  
    "*Don't be so sure, my young Jedi. You forget that he was once my apprentice, just as you were once his.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Count Dooku[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Dooku was the Jedi Master of Qui-Gon Jinn, who eventually achieved the same rank in the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/QGJdirty-SWE.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111211221501) [![Dooku was the Jedi Master of Qui-Gon Jinn, who eventually achieved the same rank in the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/QGJdirty-SWE.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20111211221501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/QGJdirty-SWE.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111211221501) 

Dooku was the Jedi Master of Qui-Gon Jinn, who eventually achieved the same rank in the Jedi Order.

 

In [68 BBY](/wiki/68_BBY "68 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Dooku having finished training Averross by this point, would take a 12-year-old Qui-Gon Jinn as his second Padawan. On the evening of Qui-Gon being assigned to him, Jinn presented himself to his new Master in Dooku's quarters, Dooku observed that Jinn was frightened. After a moment of silence, and pressing him, Jinn confessed that he was frightened. He asked his apprentice why and after looking into himself through the fear, Jinn answered that he was not afraid of Dooku, but of not becoming a Jedi, that he was afraid of failing and of not being worthy. Dooku then summarized it as Jinn being afraid of himself, of a future not being the one he wanted. Jinn confirmed it, fearing that Dooku will reject him for his apparent cowardice. Dooku instead said that it was very wise, surprising Jinn. Smiling, he would explain that most Padawans would deny their fear, and even if they admitted it, they would not have Jinn's self-knowledge. He then further praised Jinn for his honesty, insight, and intelligence.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

To help Jinn understand the Jedi Temple more completely, Dooku decided to take him throughout most of the Temple, including the Padawans' sparring dojo, and the one for full Jedi Knights, and the [Great Assembly Room](/wiki/Great_Assembly_Room "Great Assembly Room"). Their last stop was the Jedi Archives, where they examined [holocrons](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") of various eras, not to study them, but simply for Jinn to learn his way around. While doing so, a particularly old holocron, more ancient and of a different shape than the rest, caught Jinn's eye. When he questioned his Master about it, he was shocked by the expression on Dooku's face, almost as if he considered it an enemy. Dooku answered that it was a holocron of Jedi prophecies. Jinn asked if there were Jedi prophets, to which Dooku replied not any longer. He explained to Jinn that the mystics sought undue knowledge of the future which led them down dangerous paths. Those drawn too deeply into them were often tempted by the dark side. Dooku then finished by saying that is why the Jedi study prophecy no longer, then turned to leave, which meant Jinn had to follow. Jinn then asked Dooku if just wanting to know the future can lead to the dark side. Dooku simply replied that it takes more than that.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

After training Qui-Gon for several months the Council sent him with his apprentice to [Shurrupak](/wiki/Shurrupak "Shurrupak") to participate in a battle on its surface, which was Qui-Gon's very first. When they landed on the surface the encountered his first apprentice, Rael Averross, whom Dooku introduced to his new apprentice. Eventually, a [strike team](/wiki/Numidian_Prime_strike_team "Numidian Prime strike team"), including Dooku and Jinn, was assembled and sent to find notorious [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") [Bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Shenda Mol](/wiki/Shenda_Mol "Shenda Mol"). They [tracked](/wiki/Mission_to_Numidian_Prime "Mission to Numidian Prime") her to the planet [Numidian Prime](/wiki/Numidian_Prime "Numidian Prime") where she had a [stronghold](/wiki/Mol%27s_hideout "Mol's hideout") and a handful of followers. After her followers were rounded up, it was left to Dooku and Jinn to bring Mol in. Whilst searching for her hideout, Jinn was captured by Mol, but before she could kill him, he was saved by Dooku who struck her with Force lightning. Jinn later told Rael Averross what Dooku had done, but he was unconcerned.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

#### Search for a senator's son[]

:   "*I wonder if any meaningful change will come of this."  
    "Is that why you took action into your own hands?"  
    "Your actions saved many lives today."  
    "Just thinking in the moment, Master."  
    "Well, then. You're a much wiser man than I, Qui-Gon Jinn.*"
:   ―Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn after confronting Senator Dagonet[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6)

On a mission to rescue the abducted [son](/wiki/Uriel_Dagonet "Uriel Dagonet") of Senator [Dagonet](/wiki/Dagonet "Dagonet"), one of the Republic's longest serving members, Dooku and Jinn traveled to the Senator's [home planet](/wiki/Wayyl "Wayyl"). To the stoic Jedi master and young Padawan's surprise, the planet's surface was little more than a wasteland which had been completely stripped of its natural resources and ravaged by over-industrialization. The two Jedi headed for a barren village in the distance. As they walked through the village, not a single resident dared step outside of their homes nor answer Qui-Gon's questions, which prompted them to enter the local inn. Fearless and keeping his unperplexed Jedi manner, Dooku immediately asked for the abducted child of the Senator twice. One of the villagers questioned why she should tell them, to which Dooku responded by producing his lightsaber. Once the villagers realized that Dooku and Qui-Gon were Jedi, Dooku stated their intention to resolve the situation and Qui-Gon assured the villagers that they were not acting on behalf of the Senator, which prompted the villager to ask how much they knew of the Senator. She explained that the village's desolate surroundings were proof that the Senator, who might have had good intentions at the beginning, had begun to neglect his people. Qui-Gon asked the villager why the people did not simply elect a new Senator, to which she replied that things were not so easy. She then agreed to show the Jedi where the Senator's son was located. At this point, Qui-Gon and Dooku were surprised to discover that virtually every visitor present at the inn had been involved in the kidnapping.[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6)

 [![Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn attempt to locate Senator Dagonet's son.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194214) [![Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn attempt to locate Senator Dagonet's son.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221026194214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194214) 

Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn attempt to locate Senator Dagonet's son.

 

Escorted to a barn, the Jedi found the Senator's son restrained and surrounded by a droid and armed villagers. Dooku asked if the boy had been harmed, and having been assured that he had not, asked what the boy knew of the villagers' living conditions. The boy did not blame them for kidnapping him as he sympathized with their circumstance. At that point, however, a villager entered and informed the group that Senator Dagonet had arrived with dozens of armed soldiers. The villagers immediately accused the Jedi of leading them into a trap, but Dooku calmed them by stating that their investigation was unknown to the Senator. Outside, Jedi and kidnappers watched as the Senator handed bread to the villager who had given up his son's location. One of the kidnappers remarked that many in the village would have done the same. Senator Dagonet ordered Dooku and Qui-Gon to apprehend the villagers and release his son at once. Placing himself between the Senator and his people, Dooku tried to calm the escalating tension by stating that their investigation was incomplete. The prideful Senator demanded his son's release, to which Dooku responded that the young man was in no immediate danger and that further investigation was needed. Unwilling to delay any longer, the Senator ordered[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6) his [garrison](/wiki/Garrison "Garrison")[[31]](#cite_note-Insider230-31) of soldiers to prepare to attack the villagers, which caused the villagers to raise their own weapons. The Senator then gave the Jedi one more chance to step aside, but Dooku refused. Dagonet claimed that the Jedi were supposed to serve him, but Dooku corrected him and stated that the Jedi served the people of the Republic, *not* its leaders. His patience exhausted, the frustrated Senator commanded his soldiers to aim and be ready to open fire. In an effort to protect the villagers, the two Jedi ignited their lightsabers.[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6)

 [![Dooku touched the dark side of the Force and was prepared to murder the arrogant senator of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/DookuHasHadEnough-Justice.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616171125) [![Dooku touched the dark side of the Force and was prepared to murder the arrogant senator of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/DookuHasHadEnough-Justice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240616171125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/DookuHasHadEnough-Justice.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616171125) 

Dooku touched the dark side of the Force and was prepared to murder the arrogant senator of the Republic.

 

A firefight erupted, and the precise shots of the soldiers began to overwhelm the kidnappers while the Jedi could only defend themselves and watch the ensuing massacre. After finishing off most of the villagers, Senator Dagonet stopped his soldiers. Dooku, finding himself surrounded by citizens of the Republic who had been killed by their own leader, felt a sense of righteous anger which led him to tap into the dark side of the Force. As the Senator proclaimed that he would not be deterred by anyone, he was stopped mid-sentence as his throat began to constrict from Dooku's sudden Force choke. Alarmed, Qui-Gon tried to stop his master, but Dooku Force pushed him back into the door of the barn and continued to torture the arrogant Senator. The remaining soldiers were unable to resist the Jedi Master as he approached and stood in front of the struggling Senator, who had collapsed on the ground as he struggled to breath. Meanwhile, Qui-Gon, sensing only one opportunity to save the Senator's life, rushed back into the barn and freed his son. Dooku, who had given in completely to the Dark Side in his desire to eradicate corruption, would have killed the defenseless Senator, but the Senator's son rushed forward and begged the Jedi to stop. As Qui-Gon told Dooku it was over, Dooku finally regained his composure and let go of Senator Dagonet.[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6)

In the aftermath, the Senator left the planet with his son, who promised to make things right for his people. The villagers nodded in gratitude for the Jedi's efforts as they started to rebuild their village. Dooku proclaimed his doubts that anything would change as a result of this ordeal, which made his Padawan question if that was his master's motivation to take action. Dooku congratulated Qui-Gon's success in saving so many lives. His Padawan stated it was just a matter on focusing on the moment, which made Dooku warmly acknowledge him as a much wiser man than himself as they walked to their ship.[[6]](#cite_note-Justice-6)

#### Fighting his own way[]

:   "*Your ideology, while faulty, does have its points."  
    "I'm surprised to hear that from a Jedi."  
    […] "I don't condone your methods, but you had every right to protect your planet. Make sure your people don't lose heart and evolve, Semage. It is the only way you will truly have victory. I say that for all of us.*"
:   ―Dooku and Semage, the senator guard, after the latter was detained for killing a Senator and a Jedi[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32)

Sometime between [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY") and [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"), Dooku and fellow Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") were given instructions to return the body of Master [Katri](/wiki/Katri "Katri"), who had been killed in an ambush on [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"), to the Jedi temple so she could have a proper burial. Dooku was suspicious of the circumstances surrounding Katri's death, as no reason behind it, nor the identity of her murderers, was known. Furthermore, since the Raxus Senator, [Larik](/wiki/Larik "Larik") had been present during the ambush, Dooku wondered how he had survived when Katri, a fully-trained Jedi Master, had not. Because of his suspicions, Dooku believed they needed to do more to honor Katri and investigate her death, but Windu was firm in his beliefs that the rules were there for a reason.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32)

 [![Dooku and Windu were attacked by the Raxus guards.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616173648) [![Dooku and Windu were attacked by the Raxus guards.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240616173648)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/DookuWinduEnGarde-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616173648) 

Dooku and Windu were attacked by the Raxus guards.

 

The pair eventually touched down on Raxus Secundus, where they met with Senator [Larik](/wiki/Larik "Larik"), who said he was there with Katri at the time of her death. Dooku asked Larik to explain what happened, but the senator acted cagey and Dooku noticed elements of his story didn't line up. Windu shared this belief and concern and wanted to take the information to the Jedi Council. Dooku, however, wanted to follow the lead himself. They all headed off together to meet an informant at the place where Katri and Larik were supposedly ambushed, following Dooku's plan. Examining the crime scene, the Dooku and Windu deduced there were more than one attacker, but also noticed that there were no blaster marks on the Senator's ship. Suspecting that the senator might've had something to do with Katri's death, Dooku ignited his lightsaber and scathingly demanded the truth. Terrified, Larik immediately turned and admitted that the guards killed Katri, but he was shot dead instantly for uttering the truth.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32)

 [![Dooku speaks to Semage about his ideals.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/DookuSemageTalk-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616174239) [![Dooku speaks to Semage about his ideals.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/DookuSemageTalk-Choices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240616174239)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/DookuSemageTalk-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616174239) 

Dooku speaks to Semage about his ideals.

 

Dooku and Windu were also attacked by the guards, but they got the better of the men and their droids, defeated them. When they got the final man, [Semage](/wiki/Semage "Semage"), down on his knees, he admitted that they killed Katri because the group he was operating within had learned Larik was using his Senate seat to become rich at the expense of their planet, industrializing it and selling it off piece by piece. Semage explained to Dooku and Windu that the reason they kept Larik alive was to make him enact their own rules at the next Senate hearing meeting to reverse the damage done. When Windu questioned why Semage did not inform Katri of Larik's corruption, Semage insisted that though the Jedi claimed to bring peace, they were really only at the whim of the Senate, and only kept law and order for the rich. The pair eventually put Semage in lockup, but Dooku understood how he felt and decided to go to his cell to meet him, telling him that while he did not condone his methods, he believed they had a right to protect their planet.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32) Wary of the Senate as well,[[31]](#cite_note-Insider230-31) Dooku also told him to make sure his people continued to evolve and did not lose heart, telling him that it was the only way to ensure victory.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32)

Having solved Katri's murder, Dooku and Windu brought her body back to the Jedi temple, where she was honored and cremated in a ceremony. After the funeral, Dooku approached Windu to ask if he had been offered Master Katri's council seat, as rumors claimed that he had. When Windu confirmed that it was the case, a suspicious Dooku questioned if Windu was aware Katri's position was open before they left for Raxus. Insisting that he had no idea about it before taking the case, Windu explained that he believed he had been given the seat over Dooku because Dooku did not stick to the mission and acted in a way that led to a senator's death. Nevertheless, Windu told Dooku that he would speak to the Council on his behalf.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32) Also growing suspicious of Windu's elevation,[[31]](#cite_note-Insider230-31) Dooku was more resentful than grateful but thanked him nonetheless.[[32]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-32)

#### Conspiracy in the Council[]

Shortly before Qui-Gon's trials between [49 BBY](/wiki/49_BBY "49 BBY") and [44 BBY](/wiki/44_BBY "44 BBY"), the pair were invited by council member [Jor Aerith](/wiki/Jor_Aerith "Jor Aerith") to join her in representing the Jedi at the annual Coruscant [Dragonfire Air Rally](/wiki/Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Dragonfire Air Rally") in hopes of making a good impression on the [Candovant](/wiki/Candovant "Candovant") ambassador who had invited her. Dooku and Master Yula Braylon expressed frustration at the Council's obsession with politics, but Aerith pointed out Dooku's charisma made him a natural conversationalist, for which she was not.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Dooku agreed to attend and took the opportunity to teach his apprentice some Candovant customs, but while he was there, he ran into his brother Ramil who was participating in the [race](/wiki/Forty-eighth_annual_Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Forty-eighth annual Dragonfire Air Rally"). Dooku questioned why he as the heir to the Serrenian throne was racing, but the older man dismissed him. While Ramil did very well in the race, it quickly became apparent his [airspeeder](/wiki/Airspeeder "Airspeeder") was sabotaged and it crashed. Dooku and his apprentice discreetly went to see what had happened, and while there they discovered the Investigator was trying to cover up the incident. Following the man, they found he was working for a [Jenet](/wiki/Jenet "Jenet") crime boss named [Cenevax](/wiki/Cenevax "Cenevax"). Ignoring a message from Aerith asking them to return to the races, they chose to confront and captured the criminal, and while questioning her they realized that she was privy to Council communications, as Cenevax made clear she knew they that had been recalled and were disobeying order by being there. With this information, Dooku deduced that she had a spy on the Council.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Calling the Temple Guard, Dooku escorted Cenevax to the Council Chamber where he made his accusation, the Council was disturbed by this but through the Force he sensed Yula Braylon's guilt. Igniting his lightsaber, he called her out, and in return she ignited hers and asked Dooku if he intended to kill her. Relenting, he stated he simply wanted justice and placed her under arrest. Further investigation revealed that Cenevax had been blackmailing her with the fact that Arath Tarrex was in fact her son. Dooku and Qui Gon confronted and exposed Tarrex, who was then taken into custody for his actions and also for having sold out his mother's influence to criminals. Braylon's actions caused her to be removed from the council. When it was done, Dooku inquired into what would happen to Cenevax and Yoda informed him she would be taken to the [Citadel](/wiki/Citadel "Citadel") on [Lola Sayu](/wiki/Lola_Sayu "Lola Sayu"). Dooku was dismayed at the prospect of the Jedi taking the law into their own hands, as well as Master Braylon's mistrust of the Jedi Order which brought her into that situation in the first place. His faith in the order was shaken once again. Dooku was then offered a seat on the Council, which he accepted, as he felt change needed to come to the order from within.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

#### Losing faith[]

Eventually, Qui-Gon graduated to knighthood and went on to become a Master himself. He later took a Padawan: [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi").[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) Dooku maintained some contact with Jinn, who spoke very highly about his apprentice Kenobi to his former master.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) At some stage, Dooku took on [another pupil](/wiki/Unidentified_Padawan_(Dooku) "Unidentified Padawan (Dooku)"). She later fell to the dark side and was killed for becoming an embarrassment. She created two red-bladed lightsabers that Dooku held on to after his death.[[15]](#cite_note-LaJE-15) Over time, Dooku became disillusioned with the Republic due to its corruption[[33]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_story2-33) and believed that the Jedi Order had become too connected to the government.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

### Leaving the Jedi Order[]

:   "*The Jedi have been my family since I was a child, the Temple my home. But my future lies here, on Serenno.*"
:   ―Dooku, to Yoda[[34]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script)-34)

 [![Dooku became a Jedi renunciate, leaving the Order despite his years as a Jedi and the bond he once shared with his former Master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/YodaDooku-Yoda4.png/revision/latest?cb=20240612183533) [![Dooku became a Jedi renunciate, leaving the Order despite his years as a Jedi and the bond he once shared with his former Master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/YodaDooku-Yoda4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240612183533)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/YodaDooku-Yoda4.png/revision/latest?cb=20240612183533) 

Dooku became a Jedi renunciate, leaving the Order despite his years as a Jedi and the bond he once shared with his former Master.

 

At some point in [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"),[[35]](#cite_note-Count_of_Serenno-35) Averross introduced Dooku to the [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") [senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), who was secretly the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") Darth Sidious, on Coruscant after Dooku delivered an address to the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"). He then returned to his ancestral home of Serenno with Master Kostana and Sifo-Dyas after his sister Jenza pleaded for his help. Dooku became embroiled in the [invasion of Serenno](/wiki/Incident_on_Serenno "Incident on Serenno"), caused by his brother, Count Ramil, who had hired [Abyssin](/wiki/Abyssin "Abyssin") [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") to attack the planet to turn its people against the Republic. In the ensuring battle, Dooku killed Ramil.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Reclaiming the title of Count of Serenno after killing his brother, Dooku also took possession of his family fortune, one of the largest in the galaxy. Believing his people needed him, Dooku decided he needed to leave the Jedi to lead Serenno, feeling it was his responsibility after all his brother had done. Furthermore, the people of the planet had found new resources, a deposit of [sacanium](/wiki/Sacanium "Sacanium"), which they could produce themselves. The Republic offered to help with the resources despite having previously decided the Abyssin crisis was an internal affair. Dooku rejected the Republic's aid, deciding the recovery of Serenno would also be an internal matter as well. Contacting Yoda, Dooku explained his choices to his mentor and remained steadfast in his choice to leave.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Although it saddened them, Yoda promised Dooku that choice was respected by the Jedi Council. When Dooku stated he would turn over his lightsaber, Yoda told him to keep the blade; his mentor explained that being a Jedi was more than a title, so he was to keep the weapon. After saying goodbye to Yoda, the count said goodbye to his old friend Sifo-Dyas, promising that they would see each other again. At the age of 60, Dooku had left the order. Dooku then became one of the [Lost Twenty](/wiki/Lost_Twenty "Lost Twenty").[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

### Count of Serenno[]

#### Disappearing from public life[]

 [![Dooku's bust was cast to commemorate him as one of the Lost Twenty.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/BustofCountDooku-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124181238) [![Dooku's bust was cast to commemorate him as one of the Lost Twenty.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/BustofCountDooku-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221124181238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/BustofCountDooku-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124181238) 

Dooku's bust was cast to commemorate him as one of the Lost Twenty.

 

Despite his newfound wealth and power, however, Dooku all but disappeared from public life after his resignation. Due to the Count spending most time away from the eye of the public, most believed that he had gone into a sort of self-imposed [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") with the intention of founding an offshoot of the Jedi Order.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36) Dooku was, however, still welcome within the Temple on Coruscant due to his past as a Jedi. As such, he often returned to it and had meetings with the Council. One day[[37]](#cite_note-Padawan-37) in [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"),[[38]](#cite_note-Padawan_date-38) he returned for one such meeting while the Council was feuding with Jinn.[[37]](#cite_note-Padawan-37) However, at some point during this period, specifically only a short time after his departure from the Order,[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39) Dooku was approached by Darth Sidious, who saw the former Jedi as a potential leader for a Separatist movement against the Republic. Using the Count's frustration with the Republic and the Jedi Order, the Dark Lord would start turning Dooku to the dark side.[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40)

Ultimately vowing to wipe away the corruption within the organizations he had once served,[[41]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-41) Dooku shared his misgivings with Sidious[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) and was, in time,[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) convinced to embrace the dark side of the Force so as to achieve his aims.[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39) While Sidious already had a Sith apprentice in [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), he secretly recruited Dooku to his cause,[[42]](#cite_note-TCW_Lost_Missions_Q&A-42) In [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-40_BBY_Date-43) Dooku shared with his former Padawan Rael Averross that he had discovered a great power that he wished to share with Averross. However, Averross rebuffed Dooku's offer and before cutting the transmission, informing his former master that he had chosen the light and was not interested in what Dooku had to offer him.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) Nonetheless, over Dooku's many visits to the temple, Yoda failed to sense[[44]](#cite_note-Yoda_10-44) the growing[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) darkness in his former pupil.[[44]](#cite_note-Yoda_10-44)

#### Aiding Sidious[]

:   "*Sifo-Dyas, Kamino, the Clones. I have betrayed everyone and everything I know.*"  
    "*No, you have been loyal to a greater cause.*"  
    "*How many have died because of my actions?*"
:   ―Dooku and Dark Sidious[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

After accepting Sidious' offer, Dooku helped his new ally to implement much of the groundwork necessary to begin the Clone Wars,[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) even using his access to the Jedi Temple to further the Sith [Grand Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan").[[44]](#cite_note-Yoda_10-44) As Dooku understood the plan, he would lead the Separatist movement so as to generate a crisis and war through which Sidious—as Palpatine—would grow his executive power, thereby allowing the Republic to be cleaned from within: thanks to the strong guiding hand of the Sith, Dooku believed corruption would be purged from the outdated systems of the Republic[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39) while order and peace would be established for all of the galaxy. While Dooku had private misgivings about his actions, he continued his work even as it resulted in numerous deaths so as to bring forth his idea of a better tomorrow.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

The most important project that he oversaw during that time was the creation of a [clone army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") intended for use by the Republic during the planned war.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) It was unknown how the Sith had learned about the army,[[46]](#cite_note-Creation_of_the_Clone_Army-46) but Dooku would later claim his old friend Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas had willingly brought him into the fold to help establish it. Greatly troubled by the Republic's tumultuous political situation and the Jedi Council's apparent complacency, Dyas ordered the clone army from the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan"), which Dyas hoped to hold in reserve in case of civil war.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

#### Creating Grievous[]

By the year [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY"),[[47]](#cite_note-33_BBY_note-47) Dooku had discovered[[48]](#cite_note-Jedi_Vs._Sith_-_37-S-48) the [Kaleesh](/wiki/Kaleesh "Kaleesh") [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"),[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) who had been shown to be a brilliant military leader[[49]](#cite_note-Ships_and_Vehicles_45-49) with a remarkable reputation as a successful warlord on his homeworld of [Kalee](/wiki/Kalee "Kalee").[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) Dooku and Sidious saw Grievous's potential when Grievous led his people in a [war](/wiki/Kaleesh-Yam%27rii_war "Kaleesh-Yam'rii war") against their planetary neighbors, the [Yam'rii](/wiki/Yam%27rii "Yam'rii"), a greedy, technologically-advanced [insectoid](/wiki/Insectoid "Insectoid") species[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) from the desolate planet[[52]](#cite_note-English_Ships_and_Vehicles_55-52) [Huk](/wiki/Huk "Huk")[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) in the [Huk system](/wiki/Huk_system "Huk system")[[53]](#cite_note-Appendix-53) next to[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) [Kalee's own](/wiki/Kalee_system "Kalee system").[[53]](#cite_note-Appendix-53) When the Kaleesh armies forced the Yam'rii from their home, the insects took a surprising move and sought assistance from the Galactic Republic,[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) to which it[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) and the Jedi responded[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) by joining the side of the Yam'rii[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) against the Kaleesh invaders. The Kaleesh were condemned and hit with embargoes and fines, causing hundreds of thousands of Kaleesh to die of starvation. Grievous's hatred for the Republic and the Jedi intensified,[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) which prompted him to ally with the InterGalactic Clan. Grievous became an enforcer[[54]](#cite_note-BDOWD-54) and was phenomenally successful as one of the IGBC's most important resources. With his exploits having already piqued the interest of both Dooku and Sidious, they developed big plans for him,[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) particularly seeing him as a way to test experiments with technologically advanced beings.[[55]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-55)

 [![Dooku had Grievous rebuilt as far more machine than man.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/GrievousBrain-RotSVD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060501222433) [![Dooku had Grievous rebuilt as far more machine than man.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/GrievousBrain-RotSVD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20060501222433)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/GrievousBrain-RotSVD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060501222433) 

Dooku had Grievous rebuilt as far more machine than man.

 

Grievous willingly took the Sith up on their offer of cybernetic enhancements[[55]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-55) and replaced portions of his body over time.[[56]](#cite_note-SWEasy-56) [Grievous' shuttle](/wiki/Grievous%27_shuttle "Grievous' shuttle") was later gravely [sabotaged](/wiki/Sabotage_of_Grievous%27_shuttle "Sabotage of Grievous' shuttle"), nearly killing him[[57]](#cite_note-Galaxy_at_War-57) and destroying the majority[[58]](#cite_note-Alien_Archive-58) of what remained[[59]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-59) of his original body.[[58]](#cite_note-Alien_Archive-58) After that gruesome shuttle crash,[[57]](#cite_note-Galaxy_at_War-57) Grievous was nearly totally gutted and mutilated by [surgical FX droids](/wiki/FX-series_medical_assistant_droid "FX-series medical assistant droid").[[60]](#cite_note-German_Build_X-Wing_47-60) Dooku offered the Kaleesh warrior life-saving surgery[[61]](#cite_note-Build_X-Wing_47-61) and claimed that a Jedi was responsible for the sabotage,[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) which fueled Grievous to accept reconstruction and return to military service[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) with a deep and fierce hatred of the Jedi,[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) the Republic, and the Yam'rii;[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) however, in truth, Dooku was directly responsible for Grievous' injuries and subsequent transformation. Under Dooku's direction, Separatist [cybernetic experts](/wiki/Cyberneticist "Cyberneticist") and Geonosian biotechs nearly completely reconstructed Grievous. Dooku initially gave the general a [weapon](/wiki/Grievous%27_first_lightsaber "Grievous' first lightsaber") that belonged to a [long-dead friend](/wiki/Unidentified_Jedi_(friend_of_Dooku) "Unidentified Jedi (friend of Dooku)"),[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50) a former Jedi,[[62]](#cite_note-Spanish_HC_8-62) and had him spend hours upon hours studying [holovids](/wiki/Holovid "Holovid") of Jedi in battle and reading all the training manuals he could furnish him with.[[63]](#cite_note-Saber_Truth-63) Dooku continued to instruct Grievous in lightsaber combat,[[64]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-64) making him even more lethal. Grievous then modified and improved his cybernetic body throughout time and was soon unleashed on the galaxy.[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51)

#### Visiting the Temple[]

:   "*Master Yaddle is right about one thing. A Sith Lord is not to be trifled with. And I will not be there to protect you, my old Padawan."  
    "You need not worry, Master. Obi-Wan fills that role now. He acquits himself quite well."  
    "That's good. I should like to meet him someday. You're always singing his praises.*"
:   ―Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn after the latter first encountered Darth Maul[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

In [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"),[[65]](#cite_note-TSLdate-65) Dooku visited the Jedi Temple[[44]](#cite_note-Yoda_10-44) and secretly entered the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives"), where he used Sifo Dyas' authorization to erase data on the existence of the planet [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"), where the clone army Dyas had ordered was being developed. After doing so, he noticed commotion between the Jedi within the archives and asked [Jedi archivist](/wiki/Jedi_archivist "Jedi archivist") [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu") about it, who informed him that his former Padawan Qui-Gon Jinn had encountered with an alleged Sith Lord on the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") planet [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine").[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) Qui-Gon and his Padawan, [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), had traveled to the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") in an attempt to negotiate with [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") [of the](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation") [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") to relinquish his [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") on the planet. Gunray, however, under orders from Sidious—who had engineered the conflict to get himself elected Supreme Chancellor—ordered for the two Jedi to be killed, though their attempts failed and the two Jedi managed to escape Naboo alongside its queen, [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"). On their way to Coruscant, the crew made a stop at Tatooine, where they encountered Maul, whom they managed to evade.[[66]](#cite_note-Episode_I-66)

Upon hearing that, Dooku commented to her that Jinn had an active imagination, which Nu reminded Dooku he once had. Remarking that such a quality was valued a lot less in the Jedi Temple, Dooku left the Archives and found his way to Jinn, who was walking through the Temple halls with Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle"), to ask him about the supposed Sith Lord he had encountered. Dooku guessed correctly that the Jedi Council had not wanted to believe that conclusion, adding that he had been warning them about the coming darkness for years and they had never taken him seriously. Yaddle, a council member, spoke up and insisted that, though she did not doubt his claim, they had found no reason to cause undue alarm, adding that the advice and decision of the Council was to be cautious until they knew more. While neither Jinn nor Yaddle were aware of Dooku's firsthand knowledge, the former Jedi warned them, especially Jinn, to act with caution when encountering a Sith, reminding his former Padawan that he would no longer be there to protect him. Jinn assured him that Kenobi, whom Dooku had never met but wanted to due to Jinn's high praise of the young man, looked out for him. After Jinn left, Yaddle noticed Dooku appeared conflicted, leading the two to muse about how quickly their students grew up before Dooku left.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

### Becoming Darth Tyranus[]

#### The apprentice of a Dark Lord[]

:   **Sidious**: "*Remember what you told me. The Jedi blindly serve a corrupt Senate that fails the Republic it represents. Do you want to prove your loyalty? Kill her!*"
:   **Yaddle**: "*There's still a chance to make things right.*"
:   **Dooku**: "*I'm afraid...*"
:   **Yaddle**: "*I know you are.*"
:   **Dooku**: "*I'm afraid it's too late.*"
:   ―[Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle") and Dooku[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

 [![Master Yaddle finds Count Dooku in front of the Great Tree.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/TheSithLord.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194619) [![Master Yaddle finds Count Dooku in front of the Great Tree.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/TheSithLord.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221026194619)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/TheSithLord.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194619) 

Master Yaddle finds Count Dooku in front of the Great Tree.

 

Not long after, Qui-Gon, Kenobi, and Queen Amidala returned to Naboo and [repelled the Federation Invasion](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), though Maul killed Qui-Gon in the process. Meanwhile,[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Dooku needed to make certain that Sifo-Dyas would remain silent about the clone army. Acting under the name "Tyranus," he betrayed his friend by contacting [Lom Pyke](/wiki/Lom_Pyke "Lom Pyke") of the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate")[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) shortly after the Battle of Naboo[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) and instructing him to murder Sifo-Dyas by way of shooting down his shuttle during a mission.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

After hearing the news of Jinn's death, Dooku visited the [Great Tree](/wiki/Great_Tree_(Coruscant) "Great Tree (Coruscant)") in the Jedi Temple on Coruscant once again to reflect on his death, as he had taken a young Jinn to the tree often. He recounted this to Master Yaddle, who had approached him there and Yaddle informed him that [Jinn's funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn "Funeral of Qui-Gon Jinn") was to be held on Naboo and that the council would be traveling to attend, but Dooku informed her that he would not be attending, as he believed his presence would not be enjoyed or welcome. She asked if he blamed the council for Jinn's death, but Dooku only said that he had become one with the Force and it was thus time to let him go. Yaddle asked if he was capable of doing this, but Dooku said he had no other choice. Dooku then left and traveled to his and Sidious' [meeting place](/wiki/Inquisitorius_Headquarters "Inquisitorius Headquarters") in [The Works](/wiki/The_Works "The Works") industrial zone on the planet to confront Sidious, furious that his ally's machinations had resulted in the death of his former apprentice.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

Confronting the Sith Lord, Dooku accused Sidious of making him betray everything and everyone he had known. Sidious claimed that all of Dooku's actions had been in the service of a greater good and that his betrayal had been a necessary evil. Unbeknownst to Dooku, Yaddle had followed him in secret; after overhearing his conversation with Sidious, she confronted them and urged Dooku to surrender to her and help her defeat Sidious. Dooku hesitated initially but then, Sidious reminded Dooku of how the Jedi blindly served the corrupt Galactic Senate, and on Sidious' orders, [engaged](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Works "Duel in the Works") Yaddle in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") as a final test of loyalty. In spite of Yaddle's great efforts, Dooku- with his nearly unrivaled dueling prowess- quickly began to overwhelm her. Managing to hide behind Sidious' ship, Yaddle called out to Dooku, admitting that the Jedi Council had been wrong and informing him that as a result, she had chosen to step down from the body. Her last attempt at persuading Dooku failed, however. After another short exchange of blows, Yaddle retreated to the doorway leading back to her ship. As Dooku mocked her for "running back to the Council", Yaddle retorted he had run straight into the arms of evil.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21)

Angered, Dooku attacked Yaddle with greater ferocity and knocked her into the frame of the large doorway, temporarily stunning the smaller Jedi Master. Dooku wasted no time and flipped the lever controlling the door, which came crashing down onto his former friend. Collapsing in anguish over what he had just done, Dooku was reassured by Sidious, who congratulated his new apprentice. To their shock, Yaddle suddenly reappeared, lifting the doorway off of herself in one final display of her immense Force power, which sapped her of remaining energy. Lying defenseless and exhausted at Dooku's feet, Yaddle stated that many would suffer under Dooku's scheme for galactic order. Dooku replied sarcastically that he would give Yaddle peace, then impaled her with his lightsaber, killing her instantly. Sidious then formally anointed Dooku as his new Sith apprentice[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) and gave him the name Darth Tyranus,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) the same name Dooku had been using as his cover for some time.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) Dooku would come to regard it as a formidable name worthy of his power.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67)

#### Faking the death of Sifo-Dyas[]

Dooku was given Sifo-Dyas' body by the Pykes. Dooku took Dyas' body to the planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), which was in the midst of a conflict[[46]](#cite_note-Creation_of_the_Clone_Army-46) the Jedi had ordered Dyas to [stop](/wiki/Mission_to_Felucia_(Sifo-Dyas) "Mission to Felucia (Sifo-Dyas)"). Once there, Dooku made it seem like the two of them had been dispatched together to solve the crisis.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) Dooku made it seem like Dyas died in the local conflict,[[46]](#cite_note-Creation_of_the_Clone_Army-46) and the body was burned by the [native Felucians](/wiki/Jungle_Felucian "Jungle Felucian"). However, unbeknownst to Dooku, another person had been in Dyas' shuttle; the Pykes had captured Valorum's aide, [Silman](/wiki/Silman "Silman"), and imprisoned him as insurance against possible betrayal by Dooku.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

#### Setting the groundwork[]

:   "*I'm sure you'll find the price the Kaminoans are offering is more than fair.*"  
    "*For access to my genetic template.*"
:   ―Dooku and Jango Fett[[68]](#cite_note-AORJF-68)

 [![Dooku and his new Master conspired to grow a clone army, using the bounty hunter Jango Fett as a template.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) [![Dooku and his new Master conspired to grow a clone army, using the bounty hunter Jango Fett as a template.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190111035238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) 

Dooku and his new Master conspired to grow a clone army, using the bounty hunter Jango Fett as a template.

 

On one of the [moons](/wiki/Moon "Moon") of [Bogden](/wiki/Bogden "Bogden"), Dooku—under his alias Tyranus—recruited the bounty hunter [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") as the template for the Clone Army. Along with a considerable salary, Dooku agreed to pay Fett with an [unaltered clone](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett") for himself.[[68]](#cite_note-AORJF-68) Sifo-Dyas had [bio-chips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") he wanted installed in the brain of each clone, as a safeguard against rogue Jedi. To ensure the destruction of the Jedi at the right time, Sidious and Dooku retooled the chips in order to trigger a protocol called [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") that would forcibly brainwash the clones into murdering their Jedi superiors.[[69]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-69) Posing as a Jedi, Tyranus deceived the Kaminoans, most notably Prime Minister [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") and [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se"), into believing Sifo Dyas' intention, while also telling them to keep this a secret. After hiring Fett, Dooku moved onto another[[70]](#cite_note-Helmet_15-70) phase of the Sith plan[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) by beginning to bring together galactic-level businesses, as well as planets and peoples tired of the Galactic Republic, to create an alliance of Separatists.[[70]](#cite_note-Helmet_15-70) He did, also, lead the [Independent Movement for Self-Determination](/wiki/Independent_Movement_for_Self-Determination "Independent Movement for Self-Determination"), which allowed him to tour [universities](/wiki/University "University") and give lectures.[[55]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-55)

#### Sullust mission[]

 [![Count Dooku unveils his red lightsaber in the presence of Jak'zin.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Dookuunveilsredblade-AoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20251001001145) [![Count Dooku unveils his red lightsaber in the presence of Jak'zin.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Dookuunveilsredblade-AoR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20251001001145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Dookuunveilsredblade-AoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20251001001145) 

Count Dooku unveils his red lightsaber in the presence of Jak'zin.

 

As Dooku continued to give into the dark side, he became obsessed with his own power.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) In time, he became a corrupt leader[[71]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-71) but managed to maintain a positive public image on Serenno as its protector.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) In [26 BBY](/wiki/26_BBY "26 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Dooku, at the behest of Sidious, [went](/wiki/Mission_on_Sullust "Mission on Sullust") to [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust") to, on the surface, discuss an alliance between the [SoroSuub Corporation](/wiki/SoroSuub_Corporation "SoroSuub Corporation") and himself. In secret, however, Dooku was to seek out the [Kaldana Syndicate](/wiki/Kaldana_Syndicate "Kaldana Syndicate"). After a tour of one of Sullust's cities, Dooku met newly knighted Jedi Jak'zin and was invited to dinner with him and Representative [Kap Klyp](/wiki/Kap_Klyp "Kap Klyp"). Dooku informed Sidious of this complication who told him to find out why Jak'zin was there. At dinner, Dooku denied rumors that he was creating another order of force users and assured Jak'zin that he was looking after his family's business interest on Serenno.

Following dinner, Dooku followed Jak'zin and learned about the mission of learning about the Kaldana Syndicate. Dooku agreed to help Jak'zin on his mission. The two made their way into the syndicate's base. There, Dooku and Jak'zin discovered that the syndicate was smuggling weapons and were surrounded by the syndicate's gang. Dooku and Jak'zin fought the gangsters. After defeating the gangsters, Dooku killed Jak'zin and then spoke with the surviving gangsters. After making a deal with the syndicate and SoroSuub, Dooku left Sullust, all while reflecting on the growing Sith plan.[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29)

#### Forming the Confederacy[]

:   "*He is a political idealist, not a murderer.*"
:   ―[Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi") to [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala")[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Count Dooku instigated the Separatist movement to destabilize the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) [![Count Dooku instigated the Separatist movement to destabilize the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241019033343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) 

Count Dooku instigated the Separatist movement to destabilize the Galactic Republic.

 

While Dooku was involved in Grievous's construction as a cyborg and trained him in lightsaber combat, he also needed his own acolyte: an apprentice of sorts.[[72]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_Encyclopedia-72) Impressed by how she had conquered the planet [Rattatak](/wiki/Rattatak "Rattatak"),[[73]](#cite_note-Sith_Fugitives_Ventress-73) Count Dooku recruited fallen [Dathomirian](/wiki/Dathomirian "Dathomirian") Jedi [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") to act as his [assassin](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") and Sith apprentice.[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74) After Ventress [found her](/wiki/Mission_to_assassinate_Jenza "Mission to assassinate Jenza"), Dooku also murdered his sister Jenza, ignoring her pleas to return to the light.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) Several years after his resignation from the Jedi Order and the death of his former apprentice, Qui-Gon Jinn, Dooku re-entered the public eye in a spectacular fashion, commandeering a Republic HoloNet station in the [Raxus system](/wiki/Raxus_system "Raxus system") and delivering a [rousing speech](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address") in which he thoroughly lambasted the corruption and shortcomings of the Republic. In a galaxy in which many Outer and Mid Rim systems were chafing under the ineffectual and corrupt bureaucracy of the Republic, Dooku's speech set the stage for the Separatist movement.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36)
