Furthermore, he began meddling in the affairs of many planets, supporting anti-Republic coups on worlds such as [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") and interfering in the political processes of Kashyyyk and [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"), among others. He also began to publicly rally systems and corporations to his cause to become the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), and publicly spurned every opportunity to negotiate with Palpatine.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36) At some point after the creation of the CIS, Dooku piloted [his personal Sith Infiltrator](/wiki/Dooku%27s_Sith_Infiltrator "Dooku's Sith Infiltrator") to Dathomir.[[75]](#cite_note-Sith_Infiltrator-75) Dooku personally went to the planet [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") to renew the contract between [Baktoid Armor Workshop](/wiki/Baktoid_Armor_Workshop "Baktoid Armor Workshop") and the [Geonosians](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian").[[76]](#cite_note-Catalyst-76)

 [![Dooku had many meetings with Governor Wilhuff Tarkin (pictured) to test the man's loyalties.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/TeasersfromHyperspace-YoungTarkin.png/revision/latest?cb=20250930235855) [![Dooku had many meetings with Governor Wilhuff Tarkin (pictured) to test the man's loyalties.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/TeasersfromHyperspace-YoungTarkin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250930235855)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/TeasersfromHyperspace-YoungTarkin.png/revision/latest?cb=20250930235855) 

Dooku had many meetings with Governor Wilhuff Tarkin (pictured) to test the man's loyalties.

 

One of Dooku's first headquarters was established in the [Tion Hegemony](/wiki/Tion_Hegemony "Tion Hegemony"). While the sector was largely controlled by the [House of Tion](/wiki/House_of_Tion "House of Tion"), Dooku's presence ensured it became a strong supporter of the CIS.[[77]](#cite_note-BMF_18-77) During the time leading up to the Clone Wars, Dooku also met several times the governor of [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu"), [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), in an attempt to convince him to join the Separatist movement. He alluded to the governor that war was inevitable, and that he desired the support of the powerful Outer Rim world for his cause. In truth however, these meetings had been orchestrated by Palpatine to test Tarkin's loyalties, and Tarkin remained firm in this commitment to the Republic.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36)

Dooku also promised Trade Federation Viceroy Gunray that he would assassinate Senator Amidala, whom Gunray despised, if he signed Dooku's treaty. Gunray accepted the offer; Dooku thus dispatched Jango Fett to carry out Amidala's assassination. Despite the failure of Fett's mission, Dooku was able to have the Trade Federation, the Banking Clan, the Techno Union, the Commerce Guild, and the Corporate Alliance all sign his treaty on Geonosis, formalizing the Confederacy of Independent Systems. Dooku assured them that the Jedi and the Republic would be overwhelmed by their combined forces.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

### The Clone Wars[]

#### Battle of Geonosis[]

:   "*Fought well you have, my old Padawan.*"  
    "*This is just the beginning.*"
:   ―Yoda and Count Dooku[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![The Jedi confronted Dooku on Geonosis, where he was guarded by Jango Fett and an army of Separatist battle droids.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Geonosis-jango-cg-with-dooku.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170217180134) [![The Jedi confronted Dooku on Geonosis, where he was guarded by Jango Fett and an army of Separatist battle droids.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Geonosis-jango-cg-with-dooku.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170217180134)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Geonosis-jango-cg-with-dooku.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170217180134) 

The Jedi confronted Dooku on Geonosis, where he was guarded by Jango Fett and an army of Separatist battle droids.

 

The Separatists' assassination attempts on Amidala prompted an investigation by Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi, who tracked Fett to Geonosis. There, Dooku was meeting with leaders of the commerce guilds, and listened as they [pledged](/wiki/Geonosian_accord "Geonosian accord") their assets to his Confederacy. Kenobi overheard their discussion but was captured by [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka") while transmitting his findings back to the Republic. Dooku visited Kenobi in his [prison](/wiki/Prison "Prison") cell, feigning shock at the Jedi's capture and inquiring as to his presence on Geonosis. Denying involvement with the bounty hunters, Dooku instead spoke of his former apprentice, Qui-Gon, suggesting that Jinn would have joined Dooku's movement had he learned the truth that the Sith were in control of the Senate. Though Obi-Wan refused to believe Dooku's words,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) just as Dooku predicted he would,[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28) the Count attempted to recruit him in apparent opposition to Darth Sidious, and left Kenobi to his fate when he rejected the offer.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

Dooku oversaw the attempted execution of Amidala, Kenobi, and Skywalker in the [Petranaki Arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena"), but proceedings were forestalled when Master Windu and his [Jedi assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") arrived to rescue the condemned trio. Windu was soon outnumbered by battle droids, and Dooku watched as the Jedi were surrounded on the arena floor. He offered to spare their lives if they surrendered, but Windu refused. In a regretful tone, Dooku gave the order to terminate them, but the survivors were spared by Yoda's arrival with the clone army from Kamino. As war broke out across Geonosis, Dooku left for the [Geonosian Command Center](/wiki/Geonosian_War_Room "Geonosian War Room") to oversee the growing [Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Dooku fought against Yoda before retreating as Geonosis fell to the Republic's clone forces.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20241012165300) [![Dooku fought against Yoda before retreating as Geonosis fell to the Republic's clone forces.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241012165300)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20241012165300) 

Dooku fought against Yoda before retreating as Geonosis fell to the Republic's clone forces.

 

As he arrived, Dooku claimed he had no idea how the Republic had gained its army and helped command the defense, assuring Poggle that his Master would not let the Republic get away with the invasion, but eventually chose to retreat. Before leaving, Dooku was given the [designs](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") to the [ultimate weapon](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") by Archduke [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser"), assuring him that the designs would be safe with his Master. Escaping on [his speeder](/wiki/Flitknot_Speeder_Bike "Flitknot Speeder Bike") with an escort of two [Geonosian fighters](/wiki/Nantex-class_territorial_defense_starfighter "Nantex-class territorial defense starfighter")[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and his escape path covered by [Sev'rance Tann](/wiki/Sev%27rance_Tann "Sev'rance Tann") and another [Dark Acolyte](/wiki/Dark_Acolyte "Dark Acolyte"),[[78]](#cite_note-Prelude_English-78) Dooku made for his secret hangar but was pursued by Kenobi and Skywalker's [gunship](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport/infantry "Low Altitude Assault Transport/infantry").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

As Dooku prepared to leave, he was confronted by Kenobi and Skywalker. He subdued Skywalker with Force lightning and fought Kenobi, overpowering and wounding him in the shoulder and leg. As Dooku prepared to make his killing move, Skywalker leapt into the battle. The two fought until Dooku cut off Skywalker's right arm, but Yoda arrived to save his allies. Dooku, eager to defeat his old master, engaged in a clash of the Force and lightsabers alike with him. The fighting was fierce but brief and cut short when Dooku brought down a pillar over Kenobi and Skywalker, forcing Yoda to break off his attack to save them. Dooku fled in his [solar sailer](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_solar_sailer "Count Dooku's solar sailer") as his forces retreated into space.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

#### Plan in motion[]

 [![Tyranus reported directly to Sidious on Coruscant, confirming that the Clone Wars had begun as intended by the Sith Lords.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211184711) [![Tyranus reported directly to Sidious on Coruscant, confirming that the Clone Wars had begun as intended by the Sith Lords.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180211184711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211184711) 

Tyranus reported directly to Sidious on Coruscant, confirming that the Clone Wars had begun as intended by the Sith Lords.

 

Tyranus rendezvoused with Sidious, who was very impressed, informing him that the war had begun as planned.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) Dooku and his Master recruited the cyborg General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") to lead the droid army. Grievous was trained by Dooku in the Jedi arts, using lightsabers taken from his Jedi kills.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) When the [Bryx sector](/wiki/Bryx_sector "Bryx sector") seceded, Dooku placed General [Horn Ambigene](/wiki/Horn_Ambigene "Horn Ambigene") on [Pzandias](/wiki/Pzandias "Pzandias"). He also named Ambigene the [Commander of Organic Training](/wiki/Commander_of_Organic_Training "Commander of Organic Training").[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) To fund his war effort[[79]](#cite_note-Ruins_of_War-79) and gathering treasure as a war chest, Dooku claimed treasures from various worlds pillaged by the Separatists.[[71]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-71) He also stole treasures from his own people on Serenno, amassing their wealth in the war chest and using it to fund the Clone Wars. Dooku's exploitation of his own people greatly damaged his reputation amongst the Serennian populous.[[79]](#cite_note-Ruins_of_War-79)

In time following Geonosis, Dooku commanded his droid army to seize control of the major [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), separating the Republic from the majority of its army.[[80]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-80)

#### Dealings with the Hutts[]

:   "*Soon, the Jedi will not only be at war with you, Count, but with the Hutt clan as well.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Count Dooku — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/WithTheHuttClanAsWell-TCWf.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250404190521)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:WithTheHuttClanAsWell-TCWf.flac "File:WithTheHuttClanAsWell-TCWf.flac"))[[80]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-80)

 [![Dooku fought with Anakin Skywalker, a rising Jedi Knight and the prophesied Chosen One, on several occasions during the war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Anakin_vs_Dooku_TCW01.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013050743) [![Dooku fought with Anakin Skywalker, a rising Jedi Knight and the prophesied Chosen One, on several occasions during the war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Anakin_vs_Dooku_TCW01.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121013050743)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Anakin_vs_Dooku_TCW01.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013050743) 

Dooku fought with Anakin Skywalker, a rising Jedi Knight and the prophesied Chosen One, on several occasions during the war.

 

Intending to bring the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan") into the Confederacy,[[81]](#cite_note-TBotCW-81) Dooku made a deal with [Ziro](/wiki/Ziro_Desilijic_Tiure "Ziro Desilijic Tiure"), uncle of [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"), to have Jabba's son, [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta "Rotta"), kidnapped and the act blamed on the Jedi. Dooku sent Ventress in her [*Trident*-class assault ship](/wiki/Trident-class_assault_ship "Trident-class assault ship"), the [*Trident*](/wiki/Trident_(starship) "Trident (starship)"), to Tatooine to carry out the kidnapping. She took Rotta to the [abandoned monastery](/wiki/B%27omarr_Order_Monastery "B'omarr Order Monastery") on [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth") with two battalions of battle droids, where she was contacted by Dooku and then by Lord Sidious, who assured them that the Jedi would be provoked into war with Hutts as well as the Separatists. Dooku ventured to Tatooine and spoke with Jabba, claiming that the Jedi were behind his son's kidnapping, and had Ventress and her spy droid, [4-A7](/wiki/4-A7 "4-A7"), provide "evidence" that Skywalker and his apprentice were responsible. Though he assured the Hutt his droid army was mounting a rescue, Dooku was informed by Ventress that Skywalker had eluded her and was escaping with Rotta.[[80]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-80)

After her defeat, Dooku had Ventress lie that Skywalker had killed the Huttlet. Jabba, believing Dooku, allowed him to send battle droids to deal with Skywalker personally. After his [MagnaGuards](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard") shot Skywalker down onto [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"), Dooku went into the [Dune Sea](/wiki/Dune_Sea "Dune Sea"). He contacted Ziro, informing him that Jabba believed his story, and assured him that he would be master of the Hutt Clans. Dooku also had Ziro take Senator Amidala prisoner when she learned of Ziro's deal. Dooku confronted Skywalker ordering the Jedi to surrender Rotta to him or die, dueling across the dunes, until Dooku realize the Huttlet was with Skywalker's apprentice, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"). However, he anticipated this and had MagnaGuards wait for her, taunting Skywalker with a hologram of Tano's desperate fight. Skywalker fled in pursuit, taking Dooku's speeder, but the Dark Lord simply laughed knowing Skywalker would fail. However, after Jabba learned the truth of his uncle's deal, Dooku left Tatooine and informed Lord Sidious of his failure. Sidious told him to allow the Jedi their victory, knowing that the engines had turned in their favor according with Sidious' master plan as Jabba allowed the Republic to use the Hutt Cartel hyperspace lanes..[[80]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-80)

#### Negotiations with the Toydarians[]

:   "*I sense you are one who respects strength, your highness. Our droid armies outnumber the Republic clones a hundred to one.*"  
    "*Perhaps, but I have heard that a single Jedi equals a hundred battle droids.*"
:   ―Dooku and Katuunko[[82]](#cite_note-Ambush-82)

 [![Yoda thwarted Dooku's plan to recruit the Toydarians into the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Ambush_Yoda_clones.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916024458) [![Yoda thwarted Dooku's plan to recruit the Toydarians into the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Ambush_Yoda_clones.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120916024458)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Ambush_Yoda_clones.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916024458) 

Yoda thwarted Dooku's plan to recruit the Toydarians into the Confederacy of Independent Systems.

 

At the start of the Separatist [occupation of Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth"), Dooku was informed by [TA1313](/wiki/TA1313 "TA1313") that the Jedi were sending Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") to [Toydaria](/wiki/Toydaria "Toydaria") to establish supply lines to the Republic garrison and the [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") people. Dooku contacted Senator [Lott Dod](/wiki/Lott_Dod "Lott Dod") of the Trade Federation to prevent the Republic from doing so.[[83]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-83)

Dooku learned that King [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko "Katuunko") was considering joining the Republic and was going to speak with his former master Yoda on the neutral moon, [Rugosa](/wiki/Rugosa "Rugosa"). He sent his apprentice, Ventress, to convince him to join the Separatists. Ventress was able to make a deal with Katuunko and Yoda; If Yoda and his three troopers defeated her droid battalion, the Toydarians would be allowed to join the Republic, but if her droids captured Yoda, Katuunko would join the Separatists. Dooku approved of her deal, believing that Yoda made a mistake in venturing far from Coruscant. However, Yoda was able to defeat her droids, and Katuunko told Dooku that he would be joining the Republic upon seeing Ventress' treachery. Dooku urged him to reconsider, but to no avail, and ordered Ventress to kill the king. However, Yoda prevented the murder, and Dooku watched as Ventress made her escape, telling Yoda that his old master was fortunate he was not there in person. Dooku was disappointed in his assassin and developed a grudge against Katuunko in light of the mission's failure.[[82]](#cite_note-Ambush-82)

#### The *Malevolence*[]

:   "*In this war, a step ahead of us Dooku always seems.*"
:   ―Yoda[[84]](#cite_note-Rising_''Malevolence''-84)

 [![Count Dooku and General Grievous oversaw the Malevolence as its ion weaponry was tested against an entire Republic fleet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rising_Malevolence.png/revision/latest?cb=20170428205654) [![Count Dooku and General Grievous oversaw the Malevolence as its ion weaponry was tested against an entire Republic fleet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rising_Malevolence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170428205654)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rising_Malevolence.png/revision/latest?cb=20170428205654) 

Count Dooku and General Grievous oversaw the *Malevolence* as its ion weaponry was tested against an entire Republic fleet.

 

Dooku joined General Grievous aboard the heavy cruiser *[Malevolence](/wiki/Malevolence "Malevolence")* in the [Abregado system](/wiki/Abregado_system "Abregado system"). When a [fleet](/wiki/Plo_Koon%27s_fleet "Plo Koon's fleet") of Republic [cruisers](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser") entered the system, Dooku ordered Grievous to jam their communications and to use the cruiser's secret weapon, the [ion cannon](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon"), to disable and destroy the fleet. Dooku sent out hunters to make sure there were no survivors, though he later learned that a group of survivors had destroyed the pod hunters. As Dooku, Grievous, and the *Malevolence* searched for the survivors, Skywalker arrived and found them first. Dooku ordered Grievous to destroy the rescue ship, but the effort failed.[[84]](#cite_note-Rising_''Malevolence''-84)

After Grievous attacked a medical convoy near the [Ryndellia system](/wiki/Ryndellia_system "Ryndellia system"), Dooku gave the droid general his next target: the [Republic's Outer Rim Medical Center](/wiki/Kaliida_Shoals_Medical_Center "Kaliida Shoals Medical Center"). En route to the target, Dooku informed Grievous that the Republic had launched a strike team under Skywalker to attack the *Malevolence*, and warned him not to underestimate Skywalker.[[85]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_''Malevolence''-85) After the *Malevolence*'s hyperdrive was disabled, Dooku arranged for Senator Amidala to be captured while en route to negotiations with the [Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), but the ploy failed and the *Malevolence* was destroyed. Dooku attempted to contact Grievous for an update, but the general angrily cut communications while fleeing the scene of destruction.[[86]](#cite_note-Destroy_''Malevolence''-86)

#### Gunray's rescue[]

:   "*There is no margin for error this time, child. You must prove yourself worthy of being my apprentice.*"  
    "*I* am *worthy, as you shall see.*"
:   ―Count Dooku and Asajj Ventress[[18]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-18)

 [![The Sith conspired to retrieve Nute Gunray, believing the Neimoidian would break under Jedi interrogation.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923030000) [![The Sith conspired to retrieve Nute Gunray, believing the Neimoidian would break under Jedi interrogation.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120923030000)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Sidious_Dooku_Talk_2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923030000) 

The Sith conspired to retrieve Nute Gunray, believing the Neimoidian would break under Jedi interrogation.

 

As the conflict entered a stalemate,[[59]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-59) Viceroy Gunray was captured by the Republic, so Sidious informed his apprentice of the dangers of allowing him to be interrogated by the Jedi. Though Tyranus planned to send Ventress to either free or silence Gunray, Sidious questioned the dark-sider's competence after previous failures. Dooku gave Ventress her mission, but warned her that she would have to prove herself worthy of being his apprentice. He bribed Senate commando [Faro Argyus](/wiki/Faro_Argyus "Faro Argyus") into helping Ventress free Gunray, and the mission was ultimately a success.[[18]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-18)

#### Testing Grievous[]

:   "*General, the ongoing stalemate in the war has become unacceptable. There is concern you have lost your focus. Lord Sidious demands more dramatic results: more dead Jedi.*"  
    "*You expect victory over Jedi, but all you give me to fight them is battle droids. Bah!*"
:   ―Dooku and Grievous — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/MoreDramaticResults-LoG.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329115625)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:MoreDramaticResults-LoG.flac "File:MoreDramaticResults-LoG.flac"))[[59]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-59)

 [![Dooku allowed the Jedi to ambush Grievous, testing the cyborg warrior at the behest of his Sith Master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Dooku_deception.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924013528) [![Dooku allowed the Jedi to ambush Grievous, testing the cyborg warrior at the behest of his Sith Master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Dooku_deception.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120924013528)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Dooku_deception.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924013528) 

Dooku allowed the Jedi to ambush Grievous, testing the cyborg warrior at the behest of his Sith Master.

 

After Gunray's escape,[[18]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-18) Dooku, frustrated with the ongoing stalemate, arranged a test for General Grievous. He laid a trap for Jedi Master [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), his former apprentice [Nahdar Vebb](/wiki/Nahdar_Vebb "Nahdar Vebb"), and their clone troopers at [Grievous's fortress](/wiki/Grievous%27s_fortress "Grievous's fortress") in the [Vassek system](/wiki/Vassek_system "Vassek system"). He deactivated Grievous' MagnaGuards and offered an "alternative prize" to Fisto during his pursuit of Gunray. After Grievous' first confrontation with the Jedi and the death of his pet [roggwart](/wiki/Roggwart "Roggwart"), [Gor](/wiki/Gor "Gor"), Dooku contacted him telling him that he arranged for this test. Grievous then cut communications with Dooku to finish off the Jedi. Grievous later informed him of Fisto's escape, and the Count suggested there was room for improvement.[[59]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-59)

#### Dooku's capture[]

:   "*I still don't get it.*"  
    "*Get what?*"  
    "*How a bunch of drunken pirates managed to catch Dooku when we couldn't.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

 [![Dooku was forced to work with the Jedi against the pirates who captured them for ransom.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) [![Dooku was forced to work with the Jedi against the pirates who captured them for ransom.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120924044609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) 

Dooku was forced to work with the Jedi against the pirates who captured them for ransom.

 

Dooku captured Skywalker and took him aboard his command ship. Skywalker was rescued by Kenobi and the two of them confronted Dooku. Dooku made his escape to his solar sailor as the Republic forces arrived. Dooku was soon thereafter shot down by Skywalker and Kenobi and crash landed on [Vanqor](/wiki/Vanqor "Vanqor") where he hid in a cave. He next caused a cave-in, forcing Skywalker to lose his lightsaber which Dooku took, and then sealed the cave off. Dooku found [Weequay](/wiki/Weequay "Weequay") [pirates](/wiki/Ohnaka_Gang "Ohnaka Gang") at his solar sailor. Thereafter, Dooku approached the pirate's captain, [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka"), who offered him passage to [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum "Florrum") for a price. Dooku agreed to pay him while secretly planning to kill all the pirates upon their arrival on Florrum due to not trusting them. However before he could, Dooku's lightsabers were stolen from him by Hondo's [monkey-lizard](/wiki/Kowakian_monkey-lizard "Kowakian monkey-lizard") [Pilf Mukmuk](/wiki/Pilf_Mukmuk "Pilf Mukmuk"). Dooku warned them that they were not dealing with a Jedi, but a Sith Lord. However, he was outnumbered and ransomed off to the Republic by the pirates. Kenobi and Skywalker checked to ensure the pirates had actually captured him. Dooku warned the Jedi that the pirates were devious and that they would not allow them to leave.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

Dooku was proven correct when he, Kenobi, and Skywalker were tied together. Thus, Dooku was forced to work with the Jedi to escape before the Republic arrived. During their 2nd escape attempt, Dooku was saved by Kenobi before they were captured by Hondo and his men. However, after Republic representative [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") and his escort disabled the power, Dooku made his escape by choking a guard. Dooku found [Turk Falso](/wiki/Turk_Falso "Turk Falso") and and [Barb Mentir](/wiki/Barb_Mentir "Barb Mentir") abandoning Hondo and heading to their shuttle. The Sith Lord choked Turk Falso with the Force, forcing him to kill Mentir with his own blaster before killing Falso as well. At that point, Dooku stole their shuttle and made his escape as Anakin and Obi-Wan were rescued by Jar Jar and Stone.[[88]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-88) On his way back to [his frigate](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_frigate "Count Dooku's frigate"), Dooku created a [holorecording](/wiki/Holorecorder "Holorecorder") chronicling these events, however he chose to delete it rather than share with Sidious due to not wanting his master to know how he got kidnapped.[[89]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_story-89)

#### The Defoliator test[]

:   "*When Count Dooku sees how successful my weapon is against civilian targets, I will no doubt be promoted to a more, hmm,* substantial *position within the Alliance.*"
:   ―Lok Durd, on the Defoliator project[[90]](#cite_note-Defenders_of_Peace-90)

 [![Dooku approved of Lok Durd's plan to field-test the defoliator on civilian targets.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LokDurddude2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100122142122) [![Dooku approved of Lok Durd's plan to field-test the defoliator on civilian targets.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LokDurddude2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20100122142122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LokDurddude2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100122142122) 

Dooku approved of Lok Durd's plan to field-test the defoliator on civilian targets.

 

Dooku observed General [Lok Durd](/wiki/Lok_Durd "Lok Durd")'s test of his new weapon—the [Defoliator](/wiki/Defoliator "Defoliator")—on the world [Maridun](/wiki/Maridun "Maridun"). After the initial success of the weapon tested on [grass](/wiki/Grass "Grass") and two battle droids, Dooku asked to the general to test the weapon on living targets. Durd assured him that he would test it on the [Lurmen](/wiki/Lurmen "Lurmen") colonists.[[90]](#cite_note-Defenders_of_Peace-90)

#### Occupation of Ryloth[]

:   "*Your Tactical Droid has informed me of the pitiful job you have done protecting our investment on Ryloth.* "
:   ―Count Dooku, to Wat Tambor[[91]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-91)

 [![Dooku ordered the Separatist forces to destroy the city of Lessu before evacuating Ryloth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/TA-175_orders.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005171802) [![Dooku ordered the Separatist forces to destroy the city of Lessu before evacuating Ryloth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/TA-175_orders.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121005171802)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/TA-175_orders.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005171802) 

Dooku ordered the Separatist forces to destroy the city of Lessu before evacuating Ryloth.

 

During the initial start of the Republic's return to Ryloth, Dooku assured Tambor that the Republic forces were spread thin in its sector and that it would be suicide for the Republic.[[92]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-92) After the Republic landed and were moving on the capital of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City"), Dooku was informed by [TA-175](/wiki/TA-175 "TA-175") of Tambor's pitiful job in protecting the Separatist's investment on Ryloth. Though Tambor claimed that the tactical droid was exaggerating, Dooku warned him that he was no match for Windu. Dooku then ordered Tambor to evacuate with what valuables he had and to destroy what was left. Dooku told Tambor that the charred ruins of Ryloth would demonstrate to the galaxy the cost of a Republic "victory." Dooku then contacted Tambor again, shocked that he had not left yet. Dooku then ordered him out before Windu and the Republic arrive. He then gave TA-175 orders to bomb the capital after they leave. After the Republic arrived and captured Tambor, Dooku ordered TA-175 to bomb the capital.[[91]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-91)

#### Dealing with the Death Watch[]

 [![Dooku supported a regime change on Mandalore, favoring Pre Vizsla and his Death Watch organization.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907215421) [![Dooku supported a regime change on Mandalore, favoring Pre Vizsla and his Death Watch organization.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120907215421)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/VizslaArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907215421) 

Dooku supported a regime change on Mandalore, favoring Pre Vizsla and his Death Watch organization.

 

Dooku secretly supported the [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch") movement on [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"). Dooku spoke with its leader, Governor [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla") of [Concordia](/wiki/Concordia "Concordia"), about the [Jedi Council's](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") investigation on Mandalore. Dooku assured him that if the Republic sends an occupation force to Mandalore, the people would rebel and join the Death Watch.[[93]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-93) Dooku had Vizsla send one of his assassins to Coruscant to eliminate Duchess [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze") from interfering with their plans. Unfortunately, the Duchess stopped their plans. Dooku warned Vizsla that without his forces, Death Watch would only hold the planet for a day. Dooku assured him that he had other ways of accomplishing their goals.[[94]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-94)

Following these events, Dooku betrayed the Death Watch.[[95]](#cite_note-Eminence-95) Vizsla was left with a lightsaber scar on his face as a "parting gift" from Dooku but managed to escape, vowing vengeance on the Sith Lord.[[96]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-96)

### Continuing the war[]

#### Preventing peace[]

:   "*After our attack, chances of peace will disappear.*"
:   ―Count Dooku[[97]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-97)

 [![War profiteers in the Galactic Senate secretly worked with Dooku to prolong the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SaamCardDoddAndHoloDooku-TCWS03E10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170406173340) [![War profiteers in the Galactic Senate secretly worked with Dooku to prolong the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SaamCardDoddAndHoloDooku-TCWS03E10.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170406173340)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SaamCardDoddAndHoloDooku-TCWS03E10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170406173340) 

War profiteers in the Galactic Senate secretly worked with Dooku to prolong the Clone Wars.

 

Dooku endorsed a [peace initiative](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_initiative "Confederate–Republic peace initiative") being offered by the [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate"). However, Dooku had General Grievous carry out a [mission](/wiki/Bombing_of_Coruscant%27s_central_power_distribution_grid "Bombing of Coruscant's central power distribution grid") to ensure that Lord Sidious' plans continue unhindered. Dooku assured Republic senators Lott Dod, [Gume Saam](/wiki/Gume_Saam "Gume Saam"), and [Nix Card](/wiki/Nix_Card "Nix Card") that they would ensure that the banks would be deregulated and they would receive their profits.[[97]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-97)

Dooku then offered his assistance to [Pantoran](/wiki/Pantoran "Pantoran") [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [Papanoida](/wiki/Notluwiski_Papanoida "Notluwiski Papanoida") when his daughters were kidnapped.[[98]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-98)

Dooku then attempted to coerce [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora"), a moon of [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia") to join the Separatists by sending the Trade Federation to [blockade](/wiki/Blockade_of_Pantora "Blockade of Pantora") the planet.[[98]](#cite_note-Sphere_of_Influence-98)

After the attack, Dooku sent a message saying that the Republic had killed the very sponsor of the peace initiative, [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri"). In truth, Dooku had sent his agents to kill Bonteri. Dooku then sent bounty hunters [Robonino](/wiki/Robonino "Robonino") and [Chata Hyoki](/wiki/Chata_Hyoki "Chata Hyoki") to intimidate Senators from voting against the [military enhancement bill](/wiki/Republic_military_enhancement_bill "Republic military enhancement bill"). Dooku then sent them to eliminate Senator Amidala.[[99]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-99)

#### Ventress' "demise"[]

:   "*I would hate to think you are training your own Sith apprentice to destroy me…"*  
    *"Never! My allegiance is to you and you alone."*  
    *"Then you must prove it. Eliminate her.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Darth Tyranus, on Asajj Ventress[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74)

 [![Dooku disowned his apprentice, Asajj Ventress, when Sidious began to suspect her of harboring treacherous intentions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/VentressDooku-COD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923020729) [![Dooku disowned his apprentice, Asajj Ventress, when Sidious began to suspect her of harboring treacherous intentions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/VentressDooku-COD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120923020729)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/VentressDooku-COD.png/revision/latest?cb=20120923020729) 

Dooku disowned his apprentice, Asajj Ventress, when Sidious began to suspect her of harboring treacherous intentions.

 

Tyranus was then contacted by Lord Sidious about his assassin, Ventress, and how she was becoming powerful. Sidious believed that Tyranus was training his own apprentice and was planning to replace him. Tyranus assured Sidious that his loyalty was to him alone. To prove his loyalty, the Sith Lord was ordered to eliminate Ventress. Tyranus tried to convince Sidious not to do this, but he complied. Dooku then contacted Ventress at Sullust, informing her that he recalled her reinforcements. Ventress implored Dooku to help destroy the Jedi, but he told her that she was no longer his apprentice and that she would soon die. Dooku then contacted the tactical droid, [TJ-912](/wiki/TJ-912 "TJ-912"), aboard its [Destroyer](/wiki/TJ-912%27s_Recusant-class_light_destroyer "TJ-912's Recusant-class light destroyer") and ordered it to destroy Ventress aboard the flagship. TJ-912 carried out Dooku's orders and informed him that she was dead. Dooku ordered TJ-912 to withdraw. Tyranus then informed Sidious that Ventress had been destroyed, proving his loyalty to his master.[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74)

Dooku then came under attack by Ventress and her fellow Nightsisters posing as Jedi at his [palace](/wiki/Castle_Serenno "Castle Serenno") on Serenno. Though his senses were dulled by their poison, Dooku was able to fight them off with his Sith lightning. The attempt on his life failed but Dooku never found out the identity of his attackers. Dooku was then contacted by Mother Talzin, who was aware of the loss of his prized assassin, who was of one of her Nightsisters. She then offered Dooku one male from her planet to replace her. Dooku took her up on her offer.[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74)

#### Dealings with the Nightsisters[]

##### Reunion with Talzin[]

:   "*We could certainly use the power of the Nightsisters against the Jedi.*"  
    "*Such a generous offer, Count. But our loyalty is reserved for only each other. The only reason I am aiding in your search for a new assassin is because long ago, you chose to help* me*. After this matter is resolved, I hope our paths never cross again.*"
:   ―Dooku and Talzin[[30]](#cite_note-Monster-30)

Dooku then traveled to Dathomir to speak with Talzin. Dooku proposed an alliance between his Separatists and her Nightsisters. Talzin refused his generous offer. Talzin then asked Dooku if knew the Sith warrior, Darth Maul. Dooku remembered that he was killed 10 years ago on Naboo by Kenobi. Talzin then offered one of her [Nightbrothers](/wiki/Nightbrothers "Nightbrothers") from Maul's [village](/wiki/Nightbrother_village "Nightbrother village"), as his new assassin. Dooku, with the "loss" of Ventress and the Jedi attacks, agreed to her offer and left.[[30]](#cite_note-Monster-30)

##### Training Maul's Brother[]

:   "*I foresee we will do great things together. I shall teach you the ways of the dark side. Soon, your powers will rival that of the great Sith Lord Darth Maul. We will be even more powerful than Lord Sidious. We shall rule the galaxy together, my apprentice.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Savage Opress[[30]](#cite_note-Monster-30)

 [![Dooku found a new secret apprentice, Savage Opress.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/OpressTheConqueror-Devaron.png/revision/latest?cb=20130522021547) [![Dooku found a new secret apprentice, Savage Opress.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/OpressTheConqueror-Devaron.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130522021547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/OpressTheConqueror-Devaron.png/revision/latest?cb=20130522021547) 

Dooku found a new secret apprentice, Savage Opress.

 

Dooku was then given the Nightbrother, [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress"), by Talzin on Serenno. Dooku was impressed by the Opress' sight and how Talzin described him as the fiercest of his kind, assuring him that Opress would serve Dooku well. Dooku then sent Opress on a [mission](/wiki/Devaron_massacre "Devaron massacre") to secure the [outpost](/wiki/Temple_of_Eedit "Temple of Eedit") on [Devaron](/wiki/Devaron "Devaron") from the Republic. Dooku was then informed by Opress of his mission's success and returned to him on Serenno. Dooku then branded Savage his apprentice, encouraging him by noting that they could defeat Sidious together and rule the galaxy.[[30]](#cite_note-Monster-30)

Dooku then trained Savage in lightsaber combat and his dark side powers. Dooku was a harsh taskmaster who tortured Opress with his Sith lightning. After Dooku's first training session with Opress, he sent him on a mission to Toydaria. Dooku told him to bring King Katuunko to him alive. However, Opress failed Dooku when he killed Katuunko and brought him aboard his flagship. Dooku then punished him with his Sith lightning. Ventress then revealed herself to be alive and Opress' true master. The two of them then fought Dooku, who initially proved indomitable by the two of them. However, Opress, empowered by rage, suddenly attacked both Dooku and Ventress- though they both pushed him back and then made their escape. Dooku was then confronted by Ventress but defeated her with ease. Just as he was about to kill her, Dooku was blinded and Ventress made her escape. Dooku then ordered his battle droids to kill Opress, but they failed to stop him from escaping.[[19]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-19)

#### The Citadel[]

Dooku was informed of Jedi general [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell")'s capture and imprisonment in a Separatist prison called the [Citadel](/wiki/Citadel "Citadel") on the planet Lola Sayu and figured out he had information on the Nexus Routes which could change the tide of the war. Because of this, Dooku pressured the sadistic warden of the Citadel and Separatist operative, [Osi Sobeck](/wiki/Osi_Sobeck "Osi Sobeck"), to interrogate Piell and his men about the Nexus Routes. Later, a group of Jedi and clones led by Anakin, Ahsoka, and Obi-Wan infiltrated the Citadel frozen in carbonite, but their cover was blown when one of the clones accidentally triggered an electro-mine and was killed.[[100]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-100)

Despite his best efforts, the Jedi evaded Sobeck's traps and successfully rescued Piell and his head naval officer [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") and many others. Dooku was furious and contacted Sobeck and ordered him to recapture Piell and his naval officers and capture the rescue squad, but Sobeck assured him that everything was under control and ended the transmission and proceeded to prevent the Jedi from escaping with Piell by destroying a Separatist ship and killed a clone named Echo, who sacrificed himself to destroy the droids, but the Jedi and the surviving clones and naval officers fled to the caves below to contact the Republic for assistance. At the same time, Dooku attempted to contact Sobeck again, but Sobeck ignored him to cut off the Jedi's escape.[[101]](#cite_note-Counterattack-101)

Eventually, Dooku was able to contact Sobeck, who informed the warden of the significance of the Jedi's capture, to which Sobeck swore to accomplish, but Dooku reminded him that Sobeck's promises to capture the Jedi were the only things that were keeping him alive. Although Sobeck sent Anoobas to track the Jedi and successfully killed Piell, Sobeck ultimately failed to stop the Jedi from escaping the Citadel with the Nexus Route information and was killed by Ahsoka and the Jedi, clones, and the naval officers escaped.[[102]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-102)

#### Battle of Mon Cala[]

:   "*The whispering of his name can rekindle hope, and hope is something we cannot allow our enemy to possess.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Riff Tamson, on Lee-Char[[103]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-103)

 [![Riff Tamson led Dooku's droid forces at the Battle of Mon Cala.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Tamson_WW.png/revision/latest?cb=20140213183101) [![Riff Tamson led Dooku's droid forces at the Battle of Mon Cala.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Tamson_WW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140213183101)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Tamson_WW.png/revision/latest?cb=20140213183101) 

Riff Tamson led Dooku's droid forces at the Battle of Mon Cala.

 

During the [Battle of Mon Cala](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala"), Count Dooku supported the [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") in their civil war against the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari"). The Mon Calamari King [Yos Kolina](/wiki/Yos_Kolina "Yos Kolina") had died but the Quarren led by [Chieftain](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [Nossor Ri](/wiki/Nossor_Ri "Nossor Ri") contested his son [Prince](/wiki/Prince "Prince") [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char")'s claim to the throne. Dooku dispatched Commander [Riff Tamson](/wiki/Riff_Tamson "Riff Tamson") as a Separatist observer to the Quarren on [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala"). Dooku was assured that Chieftain Nossor Ri and his Quarren were with them. In return for supporting the Separatist cause, Dooku promised Tamson that Mon Cala would be his to rule. Under Dooku's orders, Mon Calamari captives from [Mon Cala city](/wiki/Coral_City "Coral City") were enslaved.[[104]](#cite_note-Water_War-104)

After the Mon Calamari and Republic received [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") [reinforcements](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army") from Naboo, Dooku sent Tamson reinforcements, but ordered him to keep them in reserve. Dooku also ordered him to continue to hunt down Prince Lee-Char and reminded Nossor Ri that the Quarren had to support the war effort if they wanted Separatist support.[[103]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-103) Tamson also received [Karkarodon enforcers](/wiki/Karkarodon_enforcers "Karkarodon enforcers") from his homeworld of [Karkaris](/wiki/Karkaris "Karkaris") to secure the Separatists hold on the planet. Despite Dooku's best efforts, his plans to conquer Mon Cala collapsed after the Quarren switched sides after learning that Tamson planned to crown himself as the new ruler of Mon Cala. Together, the Quarren, Mon Calamari, Republic, Jedi, and Gungans managed to drive the Separatist from Mon Cala.[[105]](#cite_note-Prisoners-105)

#### Dealings on Naboo[]

:   "*The Sith control everything. You just don't know it.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Anakin Skywalker[[106]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-106)

 [![Dooku set a trap for Skywalker on Naboo, using himself as bait to lure the young Jedi Knight away from his forces.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/DookuEnjoysHisJob-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122162637) [![Dooku set a trap for Skywalker on Naboo, using himself as bait to lure the young Jedi Knight away from his forces.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/DookuEnjoysHisJob-SW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121122162637)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/DookuEnjoysHisJob-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122162637) 

Dooku set a trap for Skywalker on Naboo, using himself as bait to lure the young Jedi Knight away from his forces.

 

Both the Trade Federation and the Separatist armies had longed to take control of Naboo[[107]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars-107) ever since their humiliating defeat at the Battle of Naboo.[[66]](#cite_note-Episode_I-66) This time, Count Dooku led the plan, with General Grievous at his side.[[107]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars-107) Dooku long coveted the planet Naboo because of its connection to Palpatine as the Republic's leader.[[108]](#cite_note-Heroes_of_Naboo-108)

Dooku then formed an alliance with Gungan priest, [Rish Loo](/wiki/Rish_Loo "Rish Loo") to provoke a war between the [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") and the Gungans. Dooku promised Rish Loo that he would most influential in his new order. However, Rish Loo's plans were exposed by Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, Senator Amidala, and Representative Binks freed Boss [Lyonie](/wiki/Lyonie "Lyonie") from his mind-control. Dooku informed his master of General Grievous' capture by the Gungans. Dooku agreed to capture Skywalker in order to trade him for Grievous. Dooku had Rish Loo lure Skywalker to his [lab](/wiki/Rish_Loo%27s_laboratory "Rish Loo's laboratory"). Once there, Dooku killed Rish Loo for his foolishness. Dooku and his MagnaGuards fought Skywalker, eventually subduing him. Dooku then contacted Amidala, offering to exchange Skywalker for General Grievous. At first, Amidala refused, but agreed to it when Dooku's MagnaGuards started to torture Skywalker.[[106]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-106)

#### Dealing with slavers[]

:   "*I see the queen has given you a long leash.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Anakin Skywalker[[109]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-109)

 [![Skywalker confronted Dooku on the Zygerrian homeworld, and was subdued by a barrage of Force lightning.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Burst_of_Lightning_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206074916) [![Skywalker confronted Dooku on the Zygerrian homeworld, and was subdued by a barrage of Force lightning.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Burst_of_Lightning_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181206074916)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Burst_of_Lightning_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206074916) 

Skywalker confronted Dooku on the Zygerrian homeworld, and was subdued by a barrage of Force lightning.

 

Dooku then accompanied [Zygerrian](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian") slaver, Commander [Darts D'Nar](/wiki/Darts_D%27Nar "Darts D'Nar"), and his forces as they moved into "occupy" the Togruta colony of [Kiros](/wiki/Kiros "Kiros"). Dooku then convinced the governor, [Gupat Roshti](/wiki/Gupat_Roshti "Gupat Roshti"), to be taken to a "safe haven." Dooku and Zygerrian Prime Minister [Atai Molec](/wiki/Atai_Molec "Atai Molec") then contacted him as he negotiated with General Kenobi. Dooku then ordered D'Nar to bring Kenobi to him on his knees.[[110]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-110) Dooku and half of Scintel's kingdom then demanded the Zygerrian Queen, [Miraj Scintel](/wiki/Miraj_Scintel "Miraj Scintel"), kill Anakin Skywalker.[[111]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-111)

When she refused, Dooku was asked to come to Zygerria by Prime Minister Molec. Sidious sent Dooku to ensure that the Queen would carry out Skywalker's execution. Dooku then spoke with the Queen and the Prime Minister about Skywalker and his friends' situation. Dooku was intrigued by her plan to enslave the Jedi, but Dooku's plan was to eradicate the Jedi. He also warned her that her power over Skywalker was an illusion, since he was once a Jedi. When the queen refused to allow Dooku to execute Skywalker, Molec saw her as unworthy of being queen, in which Dooku then force-choked Scintel as Skywalker arrived. Dooku then fought Skywalker and ordered the Royal guard to kill Skywalker for the Queen's murder before he escaped. Dooku then contacted Keeper [Agruss](/wiki/Agruss "Agruss") and ordered him to execute Kenobi and [Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex").[[109]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-109)

Dooku later appeared through a hologram to [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri") in which he denied killing Mina Bonteri and ordered him killed for treason.[[96]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-96)

#### Kidnapping plot[]

:   "*You should've quit while you were still* alive*, Dooku.*"  
    "*Fighting off the entire Jedi security force would've been difficult. But now that they are gone, defeating you alone will be an easy task.*"
:   ―Count Dooku and Anakin Skywalker[[112]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-112)

 [![Skywalker's interference prevented Dooku from leaving Naboo with Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Theed_banquet_hall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140117112348) [![Skywalker's interference prevented Dooku from leaving Naboo with Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Theed_banquet_hall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140117112348)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Theed_banquet_hall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140117112348) 

Skywalker's interference prevented Dooku from leaving Naboo with Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.

 

Dooku then hired bounty hunter [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval "Moralo Eval") to carry out a kidnapping of Palpatine. Following Eval's escape with help from fellow bounty hunters [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") and [Rako Hardeen](/wiki/Rako_Hardeen "Rako Hardeen") (Kenobi in disguise),[[113]](#cite_note-Friends_&_Enemies-113) Dooku brought other bounty hunters to participate in this mission for him. He tested them by putting them inside the [box](/wiki/Box "Box"). Dooku became impressed with Hardeen's performance, especially how he was able to kill Kenobi. Dooku then had Eval fight Hardeen till he lost. He then appointed Bane as leader of this team to carry out Palpatine's kidnapping.[[114]](#cite_note-The_Box-114)

On Naboo, Dooku listened to Bane's plans. However, he implanted a listening device in Hardeen's rifle case, revealing that he knew that Hardeen was Kenobi all along. The bounty hunter's mission was merely a diversion to distract the Republic troops, while Dooku carried out the kidnapping. However, his plan was foiled by Kenobi and Skywalker who managed to stop his plot before he escaped.[[112]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-112)

#### Extermination of the Nightsisters[]

:   "*The time has come at last to take revenge on Asajj Ventress and the witch, Mother Talzin. I have learned Ventress has returned to Dathomir. Go there and wipe the witches out. All of them.*"
:   ―Dooku, to Grievous[[8]](#cite_note-Massacre-8)

 [![Dooku ordered Grievous to exterminate the Nightsisters of Dathomir while Mother Talzin tortured him through magick.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Epguide419.png/revision/latest?cb=20130607042347) [![Dooku ordered Grievous to exterminate the Nightsisters of Dathomir while Mother Talzin tortured him through magick.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Epguide419.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130607042347)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Epguide419.png/revision/latest?cb=20130607042347) 

Dooku ordered Grievous to exterminate the Nightsisters of Dathomir while Mother Talzin tortured him through magick.

 

Remembering their treachery with Savage Opress, Dooku, at the behest of Darth Sidious, dispatched General Grievous to [wipe out](/wiki/Battle_of_Dathomir "Battle of Dathomir") Mother Talzin, Ventress, and the Nightsisters on Dathomir. However, Dooku was tortured by Talzin through her [magick](/wiki/Magick "Magick"), demanding he call off Grievous and his army. Dooku contacted Grievous, ordering him to find Talzin before she killed him. Dooku was saved when Grievous apparently "killed" Talzin in a secret chamber of the Nightsister village.[[8]](#cite_note-Massacre-8)

Following the Nightsister massacre, Dooku spoke with Grievous about Savage Opress. He feared that with Talzin gone, Savage would be a danger to him and his master, as he was becoming more powerful. Dooku also sensed something else coming; unknown to him, Darth Maul would soon return to the galactic stage with Opress at his side.[[115]](#cite_note-Brothers-115)

#### Onderon rebellion[]

Dooku then supported [Sanjay Rash](/wiki/Sanjay_Rash "Sanjay Rash") as he usurped the throne of Onderon from [Ramsis Dendup](/wiki/Ramsis_Dendup "Ramsis Dendup"). Following Rash's reports of the [rebels](/wiki/Onderon_rebels "Onderon rebels"), Dooku dispatched [super tactical droid](/wiki/ST-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "ST-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid") general, [Kalani](/wiki/Kalani "Kalani") to take command of the Separatist forces.[[116]](#cite_note-Front_Runners-116) Following the rebels' victory over the [droid gunships](/wiki/HMP_droid_gunship "HMP droid gunship"), Dooku ordered Kalani to withdraw what remained of the occupation force to [Agamar](/wiki/Agamar "Agamar"), much to Rash's disapproval, which ended with his death.[[117]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-117)

#### Retribution on Florrum[]

:   "*Hondo Ohnaka, we meet again. As I remember the last time we meet face to face I was your prisoner and you attempted to bargain me off to the highest bidder.*"  
    "*But can you blame me, I mean a Sith lord, what a handsome price you would of-"*  
    "*Silence. You are going to pay the price for your treachery.*"
:   ―Count Dooku and Hondo Ohnaka[[118]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-118)

 [![Dooku deployed Grievous against Hondo Ohnaka, the pirate who once held the Count as a prisoner for ransom.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/Open-uri20150608-27674-17pksj6_96bade9c.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170218042601) [![Dooku deployed Grievous against Hondo Ohnaka, the pirate who once held the Count as a prisoner for ransom.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/Open-uri20150608-27674-17pksj6_96bade9c.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170218042601)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/Open-uri20150608-27674-17pksj6_96bade9c.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170218042601) 

Dooku deployed Grievous against Hondo Ohnaka, the pirate who once held the Count as a prisoner for ransom.

 

Still having a score to settle with Hondo Ohnaka for holding him captive in the past, Dooku dispatched General Grievous to Florrum to seize and dismantle all of Ohnaka's possessions making them his own property. He then had Grievous take Ohnaka away to a prison cell. Ohnaka survived the assault but much of his base was left in ruins.[[118]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-118)

#### Alliance with Ravna[]

:   "*How many times must I tell you, Kenobi? Do not underestimate the power of the dark side!*"
:   ―Count Dooku[[119]](#cite_note-TFVC_2-119)

 [![Dooku tried to recruit Ravna to his cause, only to be betrayed by the Dark Lord.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/RavnaVsDooku-TalesFromVadersCastle2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181012222452) [![Dooku tried to recruit Ravna to his cause, only to be betrayed by the Dark Lord.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/RavnaVsDooku-TalesFromVadersCastle2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181012222452)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/RavnaVsDooku-TalesFromVadersCastle2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181012222452) 

Dooku tried to recruit Ravna to his cause, only to be betrayed by the Dark Lord.

 

According to a story told years later, Dooku traveled to the planet [Bray](/wiki/Bray "Bray"). There, he met the Dark Lord [Ravna](/wiki/Ravna "Ravna") at the [Citadel of Light](/wiki/Citadel_of_Light "Citadel of Light") and formed an agreement between himself and Ravna. Dooku hoped to use Ravna's ability to infect any living being into [unknown violent species](/wiki/Ravna%27s_species "Ravna's species") to transform millions of clones and swiftly end the Clone War. When Jedi Masters Kenobi and Gallia arrived at the Citadel alongside the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion"), Dooku introduced the Jedi to Ravna and subdued Gallia with his Force lightning.[[119]](#cite_note-TFVC_2-119)

However, Dooku was ultimately betrayed by Ravna who sought to infect all beings in the galaxy and proceeded to transform Dooku. After destroying his super battle droid, Dooku stood by as Ravna's followers attempted to infect Kenobi and Gallia. However, Dooku gave into his anger when Kenobi insulted him and called him pathetic, causing Dooku to strike at Ravna with Force lightning. In the chaos of the fight, Dooku told Kenobi and Gallia to destroy Ravna and his followers, a resolution the Jedi saw to by using the Force to collapse the Citadel while Ravna was still inside, thereby burying the creature while Dooku escaped.[[119]](#cite_note-TFVC_2-119)

### Approaching the final days[]

#### Order 66 revelation[]

:   "*Our plan has gone undiscovered, Master. The clone in question is now dead, and the Jedi still suspect nothing.*"  
    "*Good. Destroy the evidence. When the time comes, no one will be able to stop our plan to execute Order 66.*"
:   ―Darth Tyranus and Darth Sidious[[120]](#cite_note-Orders-120)

 [![As the clone army's benefactor, Tyranus was in secret contact with the Kaminoans during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200831141721) [![As the clone army's benefactor, Tyranus was in secret contact with the Kaminoans during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200831141721)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200831141721) 

As the clone army's benefactor, Tyranus was in secret contact with the Kaminoans during the Clone Wars.

 

Dooku was later contacted by Admiral [Trench](/wiki/Trench "Trench"). Through Trench's line [held](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda "Battle of Ringo Vinda") on [Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda "Ringo Vinda"), he informed Dooku how one of the [clones](/wiki/Tup "Tup") had murdered his [Jedi general](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar") in a trance-like state. Tyranus informed his master that Order 66 might be revealed. Thus Sidious ordered Tyranus to kidnap the clone and examine him. Dooku then ordered Trench to kidnap the clone. After the admiral succeeded in doing so, Dooku applauded him and ordered him to send the clone to him.[[69]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-69)

Following Trench's failed kidnapping, Dooku, going by Darth Tyranus, was contacted by Kaminoan Prime Minister Lama Su and Chief Medical Scientist Nala Se about the trooper. Tyranus asked for the inhibitor chip, reiterated his lie about the intention of the chip, and stated that Sifo-Dyas was the only one who knew about the chip prior to his death.[[121]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-121) However, the inhibitor chip was then stolen by the renegade trooper [CT-5555](/wiki/Fives "Fives") aka "Fives". Tyranus made it clear that the Jedi must not learn this.[[122]](#cite_note-Fugitive-122) Following the death of the renegade trooper, Tyranus was then given both chips by his master and was ordered to destroy them.[[120]](#cite_note-Orders-120)

#### Recruiting Clovis[]

:   "*Lord Tyranus, the Republic fleet will be arriving shortly.*"  
    "*Very good, my Lord. Clovis has blindly played his part. It now appears he coordinated the entire Separatist takeover.*"  
    "*And because of this treachery, the banks will be firmly placed under the control of the Supreme Chancellor.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Darth Tyranus[[123]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-123)

 [![Dooku engineered the rise and fall of Senator Rush Clovis as head of the InterGalactic Banking Clan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Clovis_Office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180517133526) [![Dooku engineered the rise and fall of Senator Rush Clovis as head of the InterGalactic Banking Clan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Clovis_Office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180517133526)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Clovis_Office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180517133526) 

Dooku engineered the rise and fall of Senator Rush Clovis as head of the InterGalactic Banking Clan.

 

Sometime later, Dooku was contacted by Sidious and was ordered by his master to once again recruit Senator Rush Clovis and name him the new head of the Banking Clan. Dooku then contacted Clovis via the medical droid treating him. Dooku offered to pay the Confederacy's interest on their loans as well as supply Clovis details of the Muuns' secret accounts, in exchange for him becoming head of the Banking Clan.[[124]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Clovis-124)

After Clovis took his position on [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio"), Dooku contacted him to congratulate on his appointment. Dooku then announced that he wished to collect on his "investment" or he will reveal the truth behind's Clovis' appointment. He also threatened that the Confederacy would not pay back their loans. Thus Dooku forced Clovis to raise the Republic's interest rates to keep the bank afloat. Dooku then arrived at Scipio, accompanied by the Confederate fleet and ordered his super tactical droid, [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Kraken](/wiki/Kraken "Kraken"), to begin the invasion. Soon after, Dooku arrived on the planet and went to Clovis' office. There, Dooku informed Amidala of the deal he made with Clovis. Dooku ordered her arrest, but [Separatist Congress Leader](/wiki/Separatist_Congress_Leader "Separatist Congress Leader"), [Bec Lawise](/wiki/Bec_Lawise "Bec Lawise"), said that their Senate would not approve of this. Dooku then forced Amidala to shoot Lawise.[[123]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-123)

Tyranus was then informed by Sidious that the Republic fleet would be arriving shortly. Soon after, Republic ships led by [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") began attacking Kraken's fleet. Arriving onboard Kraken's flagship, Dooku ordered Kraken to withdraw their forces from Scipio. Kraken protested and claimed that there were droid forces still on the planet. Dooku dismissed Kraken's concerns and ordered the droid to withdraw. Kraken obeyed and retreated along with the Confederate fleet, abandoning the droid forces on the planet.[[123]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-123)

#### Dispatching Serennian nobility[]

:   "*You are part of the Separatist movement, currently at war with the Republic and Loyalist systems. Your duke has constructed a base and is shipping materials and equipment to it. Because he didn't want anyone to know where the base is, he gathered his supplies from various origination points and sent them to Batuu, where the inhabitants don't pry into others' activities. But he didn't expect interference from thieves.*"
:   ―Thrawn on Solha[[125]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-125)

 [![Skywalker, Thrawn, and Amidala (pictured from left to right) teamed up in an attempt to defeat Solha.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Thrawn-Padme-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220309090202) [![Skywalker, Thrawn, and Amidala (pictured from left to right) teamed up in an attempt to defeat Solha.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Thrawn-Padme-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220309090202)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Thrawn-Padme-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220309090202) 

Skywalker, Thrawn, and Amidala (pictured from left to right) teamed up in an attempt to defeat Solha.

 

Around [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[126]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances_date-126) Dooku dispatched the [Serennian](/wiki/Serennian "Serennian") [duke](/wiki/Duke "Duke") [Solha](/wiki/Solha "Solha") to the Outer Rim planet [Mokivj](/wiki/Mokivj "Mokivj") after the count learnt of the existence of [cortosis](/wiki/Cortosis "Cortosis"), a [metal](/wiki/Metal "Metal") that powered down lightsabers and deflected blaster bolts. Dooku had Solha take over a [fortress](/wiki/Mokivj_droid_factory "Mokivj droid factory") on Mokivj and transform it into a droid factory, where the duke and his [siblings](/wiki/Solha%27s_family "Solha's family") manufactured a [model](/wiki/C-B3_cortosis_battle_droid "C-B3 cortosis battle droid") of B2 super battle droid equipped with cortosis armor. The factory also constructed clone trooper armor covered with cortosis, which Sidious wanted to use when Order 66 was executed.[[125]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-125)

However, Senator Amidala,[[125]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-125) [Senior Captain](/wiki/Senior_Captain "Senior Captain")[[127]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-127) [Mitth'raw'nuruodo](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"), [core name](/wiki/Core_name "Core name") "Thrawn," and Skywalker discovered the factory and [attacked](/wiki/Mission_to_Mokivj "Mission to Mokivj") it. During the attack, Amidala talked with Solha, telling him that she thought that Serennian custom permitted a prisoner one last request; the duke claimed Dooku was still working out the details. Ultimately, the attackers destroyed the factory.[[125]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-125)

#### Plots revealed[]

:   "*Tyranus? You are the man called Tyranus?*"  
    "*I told you everything you needed to know on Geonosis all those years ago, Kenobi. You should've joined me. Sifo Dyas understood, he saw the future, that is why he helped me.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Count Dooku[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

 [![Tyranus was chastened by Sidious, who warned his apprentice to beware the price of failure for a Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sid_puts_the_squeeze_on_Tyranus.png/revision/latest?cb=20200225050654) [![Tyranus was chastened by Sidious, who warned his apprentice to beware the price of failure for a Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sid_puts_the_squeeze_on_Tyranus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200225050654)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Sid_puts_the_squeeze_on_Tyranus.png/revision/latest?cb=20200225050654) 

Tyranus was chastened by Sidious, who warned his apprentice to beware the price of failure for a Sith.

 

After meeting with Yoda to discuss Sifo-Dyas, Darth Sidious alerted his apprentice. Darth Tyranus was told about the Jedi's renewed investigation into Sifo-Dyas and his death, choking Tyranus as a price for his clumsiness. Sidious sent Tyranus to [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah") to make sure the Jedi did not learn the truth about the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Army and their eventual fates. When Tyranus arrived on the planet, he went towards the former chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum")'s aid, Silman, and killed him before the Jedi sent to Oba Diah—Skywalker and Kenobi—could unravel the mystery. Due to his actions on Oba Diah, the Pykes cornered Tyranus while he fought Skywalker and Kenobi. As the Pykes spoke to the Sith, they unknowingly revealed to the Jedi that Dooku and the identity of "Tyranus" were the same person.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

The Pykes and Jedi then formed an alliance to kill Tyranus, which ended with the Sith Lord killing Lom Pyke. Dooku quickly attempted to make his escape, via a [Coruscant Freighter](/wiki/Coruscant_Freighter "Coruscant Freighter") docked in the Oba Diah port, but Obi-Wan pushed Anakin toward Dooku, and the two fought on the vessel. Nevertheless, Dooku defeated Skywalker and made his escape, having succeeded in stopping the Jedi from learning the truth of the Clone Army. However, the news that Tyranus—a man they knew had hired Jango Fett—was actually Dooku disturbed the Jedi, as it showcased that their enemy had made them an army.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45)

#### Yoda's journey to Moraband[]

:   "*We have failed to break Master Yoda. He is strong. We will need more time if we are to defeat him and the Jedi.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Tyranus[[24]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-24)

 [![Sidious attacked Yoda through the Force, utilizing the bond that once existed between Tyranus and his old Master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Dark_side_ritual.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224025856) [![Sidious attacked Yoda through the Force, utilizing the bond that once existed between Tyranus and his old Master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Dark_side_ritual.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224025856)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Dark_side_ritual.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224025856) 

Sidious attacked Yoda through the Force, utilizing the bond that once existed between Tyranus and his old Master.

 

Dooku was then informed by Kraken that Lord Sidious demanded his presence on Coruscant. Arriving on Coruscant in the Works, he was greeted by Sidious, who then led him to the tower's ceremonial chamber. Both he and Lord Sidious felt that [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") was on the Sith homeworld of [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband") for some unknown reason. Tyranus then allowed Sidious to use his blood to create an [illusion](/wiki/Dark_illusion "Dark illusion") for Yoda due to him being his former master with both using their Sith lightning. In the ritual, Dooku and Sidious were confronted by Yoda, Anakin Skywalker, Captain Rex, and a squad of clone troopers who were tasked with eliminating the Sith. Dooku attacked the clones with Force lightning and dueled with Skywalker and was eventually killed by him. At the end of the ritual, they had failed in breaking Yoda and knew they needed more time to defeat him and the Jedi.[[24]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-24)

#### Crystal Crisis on Utapau[]

 [![Grievous fought with Obi-Wan Kenobi while attempting to secure a large kyber crystal on Utapau.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Grievous_defeats_Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20180923184233) [![Grievous fought with Obi-Wan Kenobi while attempting to secure a large kyber crystal on Utapau.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Grievous_defeats_Kenobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180923184233)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Grievous_defeats_Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20180923184233) 

Grievous fought with Obi-Wan Kenobi while attempting to secure a large kyber crystal on Utapau.

 

Towards the end of the Clone Wars, Count Dooku and General Grievous took interest in a massive [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") on the neutral planet of [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"). They hired several [Sugi](/wiki/Sugi "Sugi") mercenaries led by [Endente](/wiki/Endente "Endente") and [Amani](/wiki/Amani "Amani") outcasts to excavate the crystal and to guard it respectively. Dooku and Grievous were also aided by [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Torul Blom](/wiki/Torul_Blom "Torul Blom"), who had secret contacts with Endente. When the Jedi Master [Tu-Anh](/wiki/Tu-Anh "Tu-Anh") stumbled upon their operation, the Separatists sent two IG-100 MagnaGuards to assassinate her. However, her death attracted the attention of Master Kenobi and the Jedi Knight Skywalker, who [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Utapau "Mission to Utapau") to Utapau to investigate.[[128]](#cite_note-A_Death_on_Utapau-128)

Investigating Tu-Anh's death and the presence of MagnaGuards, Kenobi and Skywalker traveled to the plains of Utapau to investigate a group of Amani outcasts. While traveling through Utapau's wilderness, the two Jedi were captured by several Sugi mercenaries who brought them to Endente, who informed them about the Confederacy's interest in the kyber crystal. When the Jedi offered to buy the crystal for twice the amount, Endente informed Dooku via [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") about the Jedi and demanded more compensation to offset the Jedi offer. Dooku ordered him to kill the Jedi and promised that he would send Grievous to "give him what he deserved." Later, the two Jedi managed to overpower their captors and steal the crystal.[[129]](#cite_note-In_Search_of_the_Crystal-129)

 [![The actions of the Jedi, Kenobi and Skywalker, prevented Dooku from gaining possession of the kyber crystal.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175746) [![The actions of the Jedi, Kenobi and Skywalker, prevented Dooku from gaining possession of the kyber crystal.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150510175746)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175746)
