The actions of the Jedi, Kenobi and Skywalker, prevented Dooku from gaining possession of the kyber crystal.

 

As Endente and his Sugi comrades prepared for a counter-assault to recover the kyber crystal, they were contacted by Dooku who informed him that Grievous was coming to meet them on the plains of Utapau. Fearful of reporting his failure to the Sith, Endente told Dooku to send Grievous to meet them at Pau City instead on the pretext that the Amani could no longer be relied upon to guard the crystal. Endente informed the Sith Lord that they had a friend in the Utapau government, Governor Blom. Despite their efforts, Endente and his forces failed to recover the crystal from the Jedi, who made their way to Pau City's [spaceport](/wiki/Spaceport "Spaceport").[[130]](#cite_note-Crystal_Crisis-130)

Grievous eventually learned of Endente's failure and executed the Sugi mercenary. After a struggle, Grievous, with the help of Governor Blom, managed to recover the crystal from the Jedi and loaded it onto his shuttle.[[130]](#cite_note-Crystal_Crisis-130) Grievous managed to load the crystal onto his [supply ship](/wiki/Dual_Hemisphere-Omni_Support_Vessel "Dual Hemisphere-Omni Support Vessel"). The Jedi followed him aboard, but Grievous managed to capture Kenobi. Following Kenobi's capture, Grievous gave a report to Dooku, who ordered him to execute Master Kenobi and to deliver the crystal urgently to Serenno; stressing that he would tolerate no failure. Despite Grievous' efforts, the two Jedi managed to destroy the crystal and Grievous' fleet. Grievous alone escaped to report the failure to his master.[[131]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-131)

#### The Dark Disciple and Asajj Ventress[]

:   "*Vos is a Dark Lord, as I am, and he knows better than to turn against his kind.*"  
    "*A Dark Lord?*"  
    "*Oh, yes. He has sworn allegiance to the dark side. He and I will take down Lord Sidious once and for all, and rule the galaxy together. Hopefully, you'll have been disposed of by then.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Asajj Ventress[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

 [![Jedi Master Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress plotted to assassinate Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Darkdisciple.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305012218) [![Jedi Master Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress plotted to assassinate Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Darkdisciple.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170305012218)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Darkdisciple.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305012218) 

Jedi Master Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress plotted to assassinate Count Dooku.

 

During the waning days of the Clone Wars, Count Dooku commanded an [assault](/wiki/Atrocity_on_Mahranee "Atrocity on Mahranee") on the planet [Mahranee](/wiki/Mahranee "Mahranee"), which led to the genocide of the [Mahran](/wiki/Mahran "Mahran") species. In addition, Dooku also issued orders that all Mahran be killed on sight. Dooku's assault was witnessed by the Jedi Council on Coruscant, who at the suggestion of Master Obi-Wan hatched an unusual plan partnering maverick Jedi Master [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") with the Nightsister bounty hunter and Dooku's former apprentice Asajj Ventress. After partnering with Ventress as a bounty hunter, Vos eventually revealed his true identity. Seeking revenge against Dooku for his actions against her and her people, Ventress agreed to help Vos by training him in the ways of the dark side.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

After Vos completed his training, Ventress received word from the Separatist contact [Sumdin](/wiki/Sumdin "Sumdin") that Dooku was going to visit Raxus Secundus, where he was due to receive the [Raxian Humanitarian Award](/wiki/Raxian_Humanitarian_Award "Raxian Humanitarian Award") for his services to the Confederacy. For that trip, Dooku was accompanied by his military commander General Grievous. Before receiving the award, Dooku gave a patriotic speech to a large crowd defending the Separatist cause and attacking the Republic and the Jedi. During the public banquet, Asajj took the opportunity to meet up with Dooku and challenge him to a duel at the overlook nearby. Dooku agreed but secretly contacted Grievous for reinforcements. However, Vos anticipated this and, although being overpowered by the cyborg, managed to lock Grievous in a room.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Together, Ventress and Vos [confronted](/wiki/Mission_to_Raxus_Secundus "Mission to Raxus Secundus") Dooku at the overlook. After exchanging pleasantries over a glass of [Alderaanian wine](/wiki/Alderaanian_wine "Alderaanian wine"), Dooku engaged the assassins in a lightsaber duel. Using his mastery of the dark side, Dooku overpowered the two assassins and used the Force to hurl them against some nearby pillars. Despite Vos' best efforts, he was unable to best Dooku and was taken captive by the Sith Lord. Ventress managed to escape following a scuffle with Grievous but was unable to rescue her lover Vos. Dooku then struck Vos unconscious with Force lightning and spirited his Jedi captive away to the [dungeons](/wiki/Dooku%27s_prison "Dooku's prison") of his palace on Serenno.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

 [![Vos was captured and taken to Dooku's castle on Serenno, where the Jedi was turned to the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/DookuVilla-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521023856) [![Vos was captured and taken to Dooku's castle on Serenno, where the Jedi was turned to the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/DookuVilla-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130521023856)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/DookuVilla-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521023856) 

Vos was captured and taken to Dooku's castle on Serenno, where the Jedi was turned to the dark side of the Force.

 

On Serenno, Count Dooku [tortured](/wiki/Torture "Torture") Quinlan Vos for a prolonged period. To sow discord between Vos and Ventress, he showed the Jedi Master a hologram of Ventress [killing](/wiki/Battle_of_unidentified_planet_(Tholme_and_Ventress) "Battle of unidentified planet (Tholme and Ventress)") his former Master [Tholme](/wiki/Tholme "Tholme"). When Vos initially refused to believe Dooku's account, the Sith Lord presented Vos with Tholme's lightsaber. Using his [psychometric](/wiki/Psychometry "Psychometry") abilities, Vos realized that Dooku was telling the truth. Shortly later, Ventress and Boba Fett's [bounty hunter syndicate](/wiki/Krayt%27s_Claw "Krayt's Claw") launched a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Serenno_(Krayt%27s_Claw) "Mission to Serenno (Krayt's Claw)") to rescue Vos. However, they were forced to flee empty-handed after Vos, who had given in to the dark side, attacked Ventress. Following the attack, Vos became Dooku's new Sith apprentice. Despite turning to the dark side, Vos secretly planned to force Dooku to lead him to his master, Darth Sidious, and then kill the two Sith Lords.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

#### Search for Maul[]

:   "*I left you here to make you an offer. While Grievous is a creature of limited scope, you see much more. You abandoned the Jedi when you understood the Sith were gaining power. Now I suggest you abandon Sidious and serve me.*"
:   ―Maul, to Count Dooku[[132]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-132)

 [![Dooku was taken prisoner by Maul, Sidious' first apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/SonOfDathomir3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128063256) [![Dooku was taken prisoner by Maul, Sidious' first apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/SonOfDathomir3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190128063256)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/SonOfDathomir3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128063256) 

Dooku was taken prisoner by Maul, Sidious' first apprentice.

 

Dooku assisted his master in interrogating his former apprentice Maul about his [Shadow Collective](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective") at the [Spire](/wiki/Spire_(Stygeon_Prime) "Spire (Stygeon Prime)") on [Stygeon Prime](/wiki/Stygeon_Prime "Stygeon Prime"). However, Maul then made his [escape](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Spire "Escape from the Spire") with his [Mandalorian super commandos](/wiki/Mandalorian_super_commando "Mandalorian super commando") to [Zanbar](/wiki/Zanbar "Zanbar"). Dooku then dispatched General Grievous and [Tey-Zuka](/wiki/Tey-Zuka "Tey-Zuka") to [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Zanbar "Battle of Zanbar") and cripple Maul and his forces. Dooku then contacted Grievous after Maul's forces retreated. Dooku hoped this attack would draw Talzin out.[[133]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_1-133)

Dooku, accompanied by a pair of MagnaGuards, then went to [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") to [capture](/wiki/Battle_on_Ord_Mantell "Battle on Ord Mantell") Maul and level the city. Dooku was then confronted by Brother [Viscus](/wiki/Viscus "Viscus") and the Nightbrothers. Dooku was easily able to defeat the Viscus and his men. However, Dooku was then surrounded by Maul's forces before he had the chance to kill the defeated Viscus.[[134]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_2-134)

 [![Dooku killed Jedi General Tiplee while fighting alongside Maul.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Dooku_Kills_Tiplee.png/revision/latest?cb=20251220170248) [![Dooku killed Jedi General Tiplee while fighting alongside Maul.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Dooku_Kills_Tiplee.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20251220170248)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Dooku_Kills_Tiplee.png/revision/latest?cb=20251220170248) 

Dooku killed Jedi General Tiplee while fighting alongside Maul.

 

Dooku was offered a deal by Maul; to abandon Sidious and serve Maul. Dooku refused, knowing that Sidious was more powerful than they realized. Maul told him that together with Talzin, they would be Sidious' undoing. Dooku then spoke with Talzin, warning that betraying Sidious would be a folly. Talzin told him that Sidious was ready to replace him with a new apprentice. She then revealed to Dooku how Sidious came to her promising to make her his right hand but betrayed her when he took Maul. She also revealed that Maul was her son. When the Republic forces boarded their ship, Dooku decided to assist Maul in killing the Jedi, but not before secretly freeing Grievous. Together they [fought](/wiki/Assault_on_Vizsla_Keep_09 "Assault on Vizsla Keep 09") [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General"), Mace Windu, [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura"), Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Tiplee. Dooku then killed Tiplee and then escaped with Maul and Commanders [Saxon](/wiki/Gar_Saxon "Gar Saxon") and [Kast](/wiki/Rook_Kast "Rook Kast") aboard a gauntlet fighter.[[132]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-132)

Dooku was then taken to Dathomir by Maul. There, he was taken to a chamber in the Nightbrother village to have his life-force taken from him to allow Talzin to regain her form. Dooku was then possessed by Talzin when Grievous and Sidious suddenly arrived. After a brief clash with Sidious, Talzin released Dooku's body and appeared in physical form again. Dooku then assisted his master in fighting Talzin and Maul, eventually overpowering them. Maul ended up escaping, and Talzin was killed by Grievous. Despite Maul's escape, Sidious assured Dooku that their future was certain.[[135]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_4-135)

#### Rescue of Quinlan Vos and the end of Ventress[]

:   "*Soon enough, you will stop denying the truth of so very many things. And you will understand that I am not a traitor, but a visionary! Fear leads to anger, anger leads to hate, hatred leads to suffering. But what the Jedi failed to teach you, what I have learned, is how to persevere, to pass* through *the suffering, and achieve ultimate power!*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Quinlan Vos[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

 [![Dooku killed Ventress and tried to use her death to push Vos fully to the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Dookuventress.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190915210641) [![Dooku killed Ventress and tried to use her death to push Vos fully to the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Dookuventress.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190915210641)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Dookuventress.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190915210641) 

Dooku killed Ventress and tried to use her death to push Vos fully to the dark side.

 

Following Talzin's death,[[136]](#cite_note-Post_Talzin_death-136) Dooku and his new right-hand man, Quinlan Vos, launched a renewed military campaign against the Republic. Vos quickly gained the moniker "[Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") Enigma" among the Republic media. After receiving intelligence from Admiral [Wullf Yularen](/wiki/Wullf_Yularen "Wullf Yularen") that Dooku was planning to attack the planet [Taris](/wiki/Taris "Taris"), the Jedi Council hatched a [mission to rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Quinlan_Vos "Rescue of Quinlan Vos") Quinlan Vos. With the help of Ventress, Kenobi and his former apprentice Anakin Skywalker infiltrated Dooku's [*Providence*-class Dreadnought](/wiki/Providence-class_Dreadnought "Providence-class Dreadnought") and made their way to the [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)"), hoping to encounter "Admiral Enigma." Instead, they encountered Dooku. While Skywalker dueled with Dooku, Ventress and Kenobi managed to "rescue" Vos from his cell. However, Vos and Dooku had anticipated the rescue and arranged for Vos to appear in an emaciated state. While Ventress sensed that Vos had turned to the dark side, his Jedi colleagues eagerly welcomed Vos home.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Quinlan Vos' "rescue" gave Count Dooku a high-level spy within the Jedi Order. Using his high-placed position within the Jedi hierarchy, Vos leaked intelligence on two Republic operations to Dooku. This allowed the Separatists to sabotage an asteroid supplies warehouse and to evacuate a [listening post](/wiki/Vanqor_listening_station "Vanqor listening station") on Vanqor prior to a Republic [attack](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Vanqor_listening_station "Destruction of the Vanqor listening station"). After discerning that Vos had turned to the dark side, the Jedi Council sent Vos on a mission to kill Dooku. With the help of Ventress, Vos and the Jedi learned that Dooku's dreadnought was last sighted above the crystal-covered planet of Christophsis. Vos managed to infiltrate Dooku's dreadnought and engaged the Sith Lord in a lightsaber duel. Despite besting Dooku, Vos refused to kill him and instead demanded that Dooku lead him to Darth Sidious.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Unknown to both Dooku and Vos, they had been tailed by Kenobi and Skywalker. The two Jedi Knights promptly arrested Dooku and his apprentice and transported them to the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") [*Vigilance*](/wiki/Vigilance_(Venator-class) "Vigilance (Venator-class)") as prisoners. While being marched to the *Vigilance's* brig, Vos managed to free Dooku, who in turned freed Vos. After killing the Jedi Knights [Akar-Deshu](/wiki/Akar-Deshu "Akar-Deshu") and [Kav Bayons](/wiki/Kav_Bayons "Kav Bayons") and two dozen Clone troopers, the two dark siders escaped the *Vigilance* aboard Ventress' ship [*Banshee*](/wiki/Banshee_(starship) "Banshee (starship)"). Ventress attempted to fly them back to Dooku's dreadnought but they were shot down by the *Vigilance* and crash-landed on Christophsis.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

 [![Ventress' sacrifice undermined Dooku's plans for Vos, who reclaimed his status as a Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/AsajjVentressDD-SWGoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20251205024146) [![Ventress' sacrifice undermined Dooku's plans for Vos, who reclaimed his status as a Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/AsajjVentressDD-SWGoH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20251205024146)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/AsajjVentressDD-SWGoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20251205024146) 

Ventress' sacrifice undermined Dooku's plans for Vos, who reclaimed his status as a Jedi.

 

Dooku and his fellow travelers survived the crash but the Count sustained a serious injury since he had not been properly strapped in. After navigating through Christophsis' crystal-covered landscape, they managed to reach a local [Separatist base](/wiki/Christophsis_Separatist_tower "Christophsis Separatist tower") that was built into a giant crystal tower. Upon arriving, Dooku was informed that Darth Sidious was seeking an audience with him. During a brief hologram conversation, Dooku requested help from his master to get offworld. Shortly later, Kenobi and Skywalker launched a [full-scale assault](/wiki/Second_battle_of_Christophsis "Second battle of Christophsis") on the Separatist base.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Together, Dooku and his opponents made their way into an outlying crystal sanctum. On the way, Dooku was struck by a blaster blast and was knocked unconscious. While Ventress wanted to let him die, Vos insisted on keeping him alive. While Vos assisted the battle droids in the defense of the base, Ventress moved Dooku into the crystal sanctum. After stirring, Dooku taunted Ventress by deriding her as a "grant" and claiming that Vos had much potential as a Sith Lord. Ventress responded that Vos had "bigger plans" for Dooku. When Vos entered the sanctum, Ventress confronted him about his decision to join Dooku and the dark side.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

While Ventress and Vos were preoccupied, Dooku took the opportunity to attack his former pupils with Force lightning. He wanted to kill Vos, but ended up striking Ventress, who pushed Vos out of the way. Though Quinlan managed to stop Dooku,[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) Ventress appeared to be[[137]](#cite_note-TBB_article-137) mortally wounded. Dooku then attempted to goad Vos into killing him, but realizing that the act of murder led to the dark side, Vos refused and reaffirmed his Jedi identity. While Vos comforted his lover, Dooku took the opportunity to rendezvous with Sidious' starship and fled off-world[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) upon being rescued by Grievous.[[138]](#cite_note-Quinlan_Vos_Biography_Gallery-138) Despite failing to kill Dooku, Vos was pardoned by the Jedi Council after he rejected the dark side and continued serving the Jedi war effort.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

### The final days[]

#### Assorted actions[]

On one occasion, Count Dooku [dueled](/wiki/Duel_on_Vjun_(Dooku) "Duel on Vjun (Dooku)") Yoda on [Vjun](/wiki/Vjun "Vjun"). Before making a tactical withdrawal, he was able to accomplish the near impossible[[139]](#cite_note-English_LaJE-139) by wounding his former master.[[15]](#cite_note-LaJE-15) At one point, Dooku fought Skywalker again on [Tythe](/wiki/Tythe "Tythe"), but the Jedi failed to defeat the Count.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67)

Dooku and his allies demanded the [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") accept of their conditions[[140]](#cite_note-HC_27-140) as [Kachirho](/wiki/Kachirho "Kachirho") in particular, and [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk") in general, interested Grievous and the Separatists. Kachirho was simple to defend while also being an excellent landing strip for droids, as well as being home to the [Claatuvac Guild](/wiki/Claatuvac_Guild "Claatuvac Guild") Archives, which contained many unknown space roads.[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) After growing weary of waiting for a decision that would benefit him, Grievous ordered to plan a large-scale attack in hopes that the threat would "persuade" the Wookiees to accept their conditions.[[140]](#cite_note-HC_27-140) The decision, however, turned out to be a dire mistake for the Confederacy,[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) and the Wookiees responded angrily, declaring an all-out war on the forces threatening to attack them.[[140]](#cite_note-HC_27-140)

#### Death[]

:   "*You did well, Anakin. He was too dangerous to be kept alive.*"  
    "*Yes, but he was an unarmed prisoner. I shouldn't have done that. It's not the Jedi way.*"  
    "*It is only natural. He cut off your arm, and you wanted revenge.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Anakin Skywalker, on Count Dooku's death[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

Later, Dooku became a part of Sidious' plan to capture Palpatine during the Battle of Coruscant. However, Dooku was unaware that Sidious' true intentions were for Anakin to kill him and replace him as Sidious' apprentice, as Sidious felt it was time for Anakin to be his apprentice, as well as that Dooku no longer served a purpose.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) Dooku then informed Grievous of the impending news[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) that the CIS had a chance of recovery and victory.[[142]](#cite_note-Palpatine-142) Grievous' fleet was able to leap directly from the Outer Rim to Coruscant thanks to Darth Sidious, who had obtained the coordinates[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) and provided them a plan to kidnap the Supreme Chancellor of the Republic. Earlier, Dooku had relocated his command post to Grievous' flagship, the *[Invisible Hand](/wiki/Invisible_Hand "Invisible Hand")*. This allowed him to stay close to Grievous and ensure that his orders were followed. Sidious wanted to avoid any setbacks in his plans, despite the cyborg general posing no threat to him.[[142]](#cite_note-Palpatine-142)

 [![Dooku was disarmed and executed by Skywalker during the Battle of Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210063803) [![Dooku was disarmed and executed by Skywalker during the Battle of Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130210063803)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/DookuBeheading-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210063803) 

Dooku was disarmed and executed by Skywalker during the Battle of Coruscant.

 

Count Dooku held Chancellor Palpatine captive aboard General Grievous' flagship, the *Invisible Hand*, after the Kaleesh General abducted him[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) and took him to the [communications tower](/wiki/Wizard%27s_Tower "Wizard's Tower").[[143]](#cite_note-Ship_I-143) After completing this mission successfully, Dooku ordered Grievous to remain in orbit and attack the Republic fleet in close combat.[[144]](#cite_note-Battles-144) He proclaimed to a stunned galaxy that the Republic leader was his hostage.[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) When Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi made their way to the bridge where the Chancellor was being held in an attempt to rescue him, Dooku arrived and confronted the two Jedi, flanked by two super battle droids, demanding the Jedi to surrender their sabers. He then engaged them in a brief, but fierce lightsaber duel.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

During the duel, Dooku defeated Kenobi, who was incapacitated and knocked unconscious when the Count used the Force to pin Kenobi to the ground with a metal balcony. He then took the opportunity to mock and goad Skywalker, saying that the young Jedi knight had great fear, hate and anger in him, but was refusing to use them. However, Dooku was soon overpowered by an angered Skywalker, who, with one slash of his lightsaber, severed both the Count's hands at the wrists. Skywalker then caught Dooku's lightsaber out of the air and crossed it with his own blade at the Count's throat. Palpatine praised Anakin, but then betrayed Dooku by telling Anakin to kill him. Shocked and horrified by his master's command, he looked at Sidious, only to be met with a sinister smile from his master. Dooku finally understood that he had been tool of Sidious from the start to be inevitably replaced just as Maul and the late Mother Talzin had warned him. Despite realizing he had been duped by Sidious, he remained silent. Skywalker was initially hesitant to kill Dooku because killing an unarmed prisoner was not the Jedi way. However, when Palpatine ordered Skywalker to kill Dooku, he pulled the two lightsabers apart, decapitating the leader of the Confederacy.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

### Legacy[]

#### Replaced[]

:   "*At the time I thought Dooku was an old fool. But now, now I see he and I are the same. One step behind. The dark side has never been stronger.*"
:   ―Maul after learning about Dooku's death[[145]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-145)

 [![Grievous was confident in his combat skills, having learned the Jedi art of lightsaber combat from the late Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) [![Grievous was confident in his combat skills, having learned the Jedi art of lightsaber combat from the late Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130215052829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) 

Grievous was confident in his combat skills, having learned the Jedi art of lightsaber combat from the late Count Dooku.

 

After Dooku's corpse fell to the ground, Anakin almost immediately expressed regret over his un-Jedi-like action, but Palpatine assured and congratulated Anakin, stating that Dooku was too dangerous to be kept alive. Palpatine further told Anakin that Dooku severed his arm and he wanted revenge, much as he had with the loss of his mother to the [Tusken Raiders](/wiki/Tusken_Raider "Tusken Raider").[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

After Dooku had led the Republic into Grievous' home on Vassek,[[59]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-59) it was a treachery that the cyborg was not likely to forgive.[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) With Dooku dead, Grievous succeeded him as Head of State,[[146]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-146) and while he had always been in charge of the droid army,[[147]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-147) he had complete control over Separatist forces[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) as both the military and political head.[[148]](#cite_note-Confronting_General_Grievous-148) He still remained subservient to Sidious and was now ordered to return to Utapau[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) in the Outer Rim[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) and safeguard the safety of the increasingly irrelevant [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council")[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) by transferring them to the [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") planet [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). The general asked Sidious if Dooku's death had an affect on the coming conclusion,[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) but Sidious seemed unconcerned,[[149]](#cite_note-ROTS_Read-Along-149) assuring Grievous that his death was a necessary loss and that he would soon have a new, younger, and more powerful apprentice.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) In addition, Sidious advised him to stay on Utapau until the new apprentice had joined their cause, as he didn't want to waste any time before finding a successor.[[150]](#cite_note-Cyborg_and_Jedi-150)

With Dooku's death by Anakin's hand, the Jedi were deprived of a crucial link to unraveling the mystery of Darth Sidious, as there was no longer any possibility of learning more via Dooku, and Ahsoka's quest to capture Maul was thought to be the next option.[[145]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-145) Grievous and the Separatist council were then betrayed by Sidious, as he had been.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) Sidious baited Grievous to lure Kenobi's attention away from Coruscant and Anakin, as his plans progressed.[[151]](#cite_note-HC_24-151) Dooku's recent death took on a new feeling of urgency to the task of capturing[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) or killing[[152]](#cite_note-Aftermath-152) Grievous that had previously been tried.[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) After Obi-Wan Kenobi revealed himself, the overconfident cyborg boasted that he had been trained in the Jedi art by the late Count Dooku,[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) but that did not mean he regretted the count's death,[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) and then he engaged with Kenobi for the final time, as the [duel resulted](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") in Grievous being killed by his [own blaster](/wiki/Grievance_Striker "Grievance Striker") on Utapau. As Confederate Head of State and commander of the droid army, Gunray took over from Grievous[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) and believed that, with both Separatist leaders dead, the war was in his favor[[51]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-51) and more power would be his.[[153]](#cite_note-Ships_and_Vehicles_33-153)

 [![Anakin's betrayal of Windu and fall to the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/MaceWinduDeath-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130209070824) [![Anakin's betrayal of Windu and fall to the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/MaceWinduDeath-ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20130209070824)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/MaceWinduDeath-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130209070824) 

Anakin's betrayal of Windu and fall to the dark side.

 

Not long after, Skywalker replaced Dooku at Sidious' side after he [fell](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") to the dark side and became Darth Vader. In the [Mustafarian mining facility](/wiki/Klegger_Corp_Mining_Facility "Klegger Corp Mining Facility") on Mustafar, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker [dueled each other](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") and made their way into the [war room](/wiki/Separatist_Council_war_room "Separatist Council war room") and momentarily into a nearby [conference room](/wiki/Separatist_Council_Conference_Room "Separatist Council Conference Room"). During the duel with his former apprentice,[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) feeling his former friend's focused hatred was horrifying, as Kenobi had felt it from Dooku, Maul, Opress, and Ventress.[[141]](#cite_note-End_of_the_Clone_Wars-141) Sidious then issued order 66, causing the biochips that Tyranus had implanted in the Clones' brains, to activate and brainwash them into turning on the Jedi, ultimately leading to the defeat and [near destruction](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi Order and [destruction of the Separatists](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar").[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

During the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore"), Dooku's Sith predecessor Maul confessed to his followers that he had originally viewed the Count as nothing more than an old fool. In the wake of Sidious' grand plan coming to fruition, however, Maul mused that Dooku and himself were the same, pawns of their master who were always one step behind after the renegade Sith Lord learnt about his successor's death.[[145]](#cite_note-The_Phantom_Apprentice-145)

#### Plundered and propagandized[]

:   "*Dooku was right in the end. He knew the Republic was corrupt, that it would collapse and become something worse. He saw it coming. The Galactic Empire.*"
:   ―Desix Governor Tawni Ames[[154]](#cite_note-Solitary_Clone-154)

 [![Dooku's castle was left abandoned and plundered during the Imperial Era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Throne-Room-Skirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20230119161441) [![Dooku's castle was left abandoned and plundered during the Imperial Era.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Throne-Room-Skirmish.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20230119161441)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Throne-Room-Skirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20230119161441) 

Dooku's castle was left abandoned and plundered during the Imperial Era.

 

Following the [end](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") of the Clone Wars, the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") [bombarded](/wiki/Bombardment_of_Serenno "Bombardment of Serenno") Dooku's homeworld of Serenno and led an effort at the Count's castle to seize the contents of a [war chest](/wiki/Dooku%27s_war_chest "Dooku's war chest") containing valuables and artifacts, at least some of which Dooku had pilfered from his own people. The renegade [commando](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") squadron [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99") attempted to secure the cache themselves, but were fended off by the Empire.[[79]](#cite_note-Ruins_of_War-79) Despite his crimes, Dooku's ideals continued to inspire [Separatist holdouts](/wiki/Separatist_holdouts "Separatist holdouts"), including the [group](/wiki/Desix_Separatist_holdout "Desix Separatist holdout") led by Governor [Tawni Ames](/wiki/Tawni_Ames "Tawni Ames") on the planet [Desix](/wiki/Desix "Desix"). Recognizing the Empire as nothing more than a worse version of the corrupt Republic Dooku had spoke of, she refused to submit and fought for her planet's independence. Her efforts ended in death at the hands of a [squad](/wiki/Crosshair_and_Cody%27s_team "Crosshair and Cody's team") of [clone stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") led by [Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody").[[154]](#cite_note-Solitary_Clone-154)

The newly-created [Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") conducted loyalty purges, during which much Separatist [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") material featuring Dooku was destroyed. However, rare specimens of [Ansibella Dellu](/wiki/Ansibella_Dellu "Ansibella Dellu")'s [work-in-progress poster](/wiki/Count_Dooku:_Words_of_Truth "Count Dooku: Words of Truth") survived.[[13]](#cite_note-Propaganda-13) Speculation began to circulate after the war's end that Dooku had in fact never left the Jedi Order despite their claims to the contrary.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36) Indeed, Palpatine claimed that the Jedi Order had been behind the crises of the late Republic Era,[[155]](#cite_note-Launchpad229-155) such as the emergence of the Separatist Alliance; Mas Amedda would claim in a [celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order](/wiki/Celebration_marking_the_eradication_of_the_Jedi_Order "Celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order") that the "Separatist plots" that had rocked the Republic had been devised by the Jedi as part of their coup.[[156]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-156) This rumor bolstered the idea that the Jedi had been traitors to the Republic since before the start of the war, but some, amongst them Governor Tarkin, remained skeptical.[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36)

 [![With his Sith persona a secret to the galaxy at large, Dooku's public words and the ideal expressed by his Confederacy persisted for years to come in the form of Separatist Holdouts.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/DSquadAgamar.png/revision/latest?cb=20200112060622) [![With his Sith persona a secret to the galaxy at large, Dooku's public words and the ideal expressed by his Confederacy persisted for years to come in the form of Separatist Holdouts.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/DSquadAgamar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20200112060622)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/DSquadAgamar.png/revision/latest?cb=20200112060622) 

With his Sith persona a secret to the galaxy at large, Dooku's public words and the ideal expressed by his Confederacy persisted for years to come in the form of Separatist Holdouts.

 

Dooku was mentioned in the display for the Clone Wars in the [Emperor's Museum](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Museum "Emperor's Museum") on Coruscant.[[157]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-157) In [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"),[[158]](#cite_note-LPOA_Date-158) the [Apprentice Legislator](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislator "Apprentice Legislator") and Princess of Alderaan [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") saw the display, shortly after discovering her parents involvement with the growing rebellion, while visiting the museum with the rest of the [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature"). The docent of the Emperor's Museum claimed that although Dooku acted out of "craven ambition" with no regard to the lives lost, he was correct about how the Republic had become rotten at its core and no longer governed by law, order and discipline.[[157]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-157)

In later years, Sidious likened Tyranus to a [proton torpedo](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo"), as he served his purpose and then was gone, assuring Vader that he had him, a superior candidate, in mind.[[159]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_20-159) While having a Force vision surrounding [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), Sidious appreciated that he was a simple boy who did not look like an "old wizard" just as Tyranus.[[160]](#cite_note-Disturbance-160) After Vader [faced](/wiki/Duel_on_the_Vermillion "Duel on the Vermillion") [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra") of [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), who was trained in the arts of Sith combat by one of Darth Sidious' apprentices, Sidious knew Tyranus was not behind her training as Qi'ra did not have a royal background. Instead, he quickly realized Maul had been behind her training.[[161]](#cite_note-CR_5-161)

During the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), after Darth Vader's son Luke Skywalker defeated Vader out of anger and hate for threatening his sister [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"). Luke cut off the same hand Vader lost a long time ago when he faced Count Dooku as Anakin Skywalker before repeating the same fate. Emperor Palpatine ordered Luke to take his father's place by executing him, thereby betraying Vader much like how he betrayed Dooku when he had him executed by Anakin. Vader now realizes that he, Dooku and Maul were just pawns of Sidious, who used them to gain power for himself. However, Vader would reform back to Anakin Skywalker one last time when he destroys Palpatine to save his son from being tortured, while also avenging the death of his former nemesis.[[162]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-162)

#### Lasting impact[]

:   "*Separatist is a pejorative term. I support democracy. Count Dooku was a visionary. He was cut short in his prime by the Jedi enforcer—*"
:   ―Helgait[[163]](#cite_note-TM-C22:GfH-163)

 [![Skywalker succeeded Darth Tyranus as Sidious' apprentice, becoming the Sith Lord Darth Vader, and enforced the Galactic Empire they forged.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/NoSurvivors-HiddenEmpire4.png/revision/latest?cb=20231103144208) [![Skywalker succeeded Darth Tyranus as Sidious' apprentice, becoming the Sith Lord Darth Vader, and enforced the Galactic Empire they forged.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/NoSurvivors-HiddenEmpire4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231103144208)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/NoSurvivors-HiddenEmpire4.png/revision/latest?cb=20231103144208) 

Skywalker succeeded Darth Tyranus as Sidious' apprentice, becoming the Sith Lord Darth Vader, and enforced the Galactic Empire they forged.

 

In the [years following](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") the [fall](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") of the Galactic Empire, Jedi Master Luke Skywalker traveled the galaxy to rediscover the history of the Jedi Order that had been suppressed by the Empire.[[164]](#cite_note-LJVD-164) In his search for knowledge, Skywalker became aware of Dooku. During his self-imposed exile on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"), Skywalker wrote a book he titled *[The Secrets of the Jedi](/wiki/The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi "The Secrets of the Jedi")*, which chronicled the information he had learnt on his travels. In the book, Skywalker included an illustration depicting Dooku along with information pertaining to the Sith Lord. Skywalker wrote about Dooku's reasoning for leaving the Jedi Order as well as his instrumental role in Sidious' conspiracy. Skywalker described Dooku's death at the hands of his father as an execution in cold blood.[[165]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-165)

In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[166]](#cite_note-TM_Date-166) [Commissioner](/wiki/Commissioner "Commissioner") [Helgait](/wiki/Helgait "Helgait") of [Plazir-15](/wiki/Plazir-15 "Plazir-15"), a former Separatist supporter, decided to employ a tempered batch of [Nepenthé](/wiki/Nepenth%C3%A9 "Nepenthé") [lubricant](/wiki/Lubricant "Lubricant") to reset all reprogrammed battle droids now serving Plazir-15's population back into their attack mode to kill the planet's population. When confronted by [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin") and [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze"), Helgait cited Dooku as a "visionary" who was cut short in his prime by the Jedi.[[163]](#cite_note-TM-C22:GfH-163)

[Fifty years](/wiki/31_ABY "31 ABY") after Dooku's death, a treasure hunt known as the [Hunt for Dooku's Treasure](/wiki/Hunt_for_Dooku%27s_Treasure "Hunt for Dooku's Treasure") occurred on [Ponemah Terminal](/wiki/Ponemah_Terminal "Ponemah Terminal"). Those taking part hoped to find kyber crystals, but were surprised to find the treasure was a clone trooper who had been held captive for the last 50 years. The trooper, [Kix](/wiki/Kix "Kix"), had learned the truth of Order 66 after being confronted about it by his fellow clone trooper friend Fives. Kix was saved by the [pirate crew](/wiki/Sidon_Ithano%27s_pirate_crew "Sidon Ithano's pirate crew") of [Sidon Ithano](/wiki/Sidon_Ithano "Sidon Ithano") and joined the crew.[[167]](#cite_note-Lost_Treasure-167) Years later, Dooku was mentioned in the *[Galactic Explorer's Guide](/wiki/Galactic_Explorer%27s_Guide "Galactic Explorer's Guide")*, a survival guide written by Hondo Ohnaka and [DK-RA-43](/wiki/DK-RA-43 "DK-RA-43").[[168]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-168) Dooku's Sith loyalties were discovered in the records of the [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") of the Sith planet [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"), which was the location of Sidious's ultimate defeat in the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") and a site of interest to historians under the [Exegol Excavation Project](/wiki/Exegol_Excavation_Project "Exegol Excavation Project"). With the recovered information revealing Dooku's hidden nature as Darth Tyranus, historian [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") published the information to the wider galaxy as part of his book *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire").[[169]](#cite_note-RiseFall-169)*

## Personality and traits[]

:   "*I sense great fear in you, Skywalker. You have hate. You have anger. But you don't* use *them.*"
:   ―Dooku duels Anakin Skywalker[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

 [![Dooku was a charismatic statesman deft at manipulation and deception.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Boundless_Ambition_SWDA.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209235806) [![Dooku was a charismatic statesman deft at manipulation and deception.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Boundless_Ambition_SWDA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190209235806)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Boundless_Ambition_SWDA.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209235806) 

Dooku was a charismatic statesman deft at manipulation and deception.

 

Dooku was an aging [human](/wiki/Human "Human") male who had light skin, [brown](/wiki/Color "Color") [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye"), white [hair](/wiki/Hair "Hair"),[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and a height of 1.96 [meters](/wiki/Meter "Meter").[[1]](#cite_note-SWEDooku-1) In his younger years, his hair was black.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) He was a connoisseur of [wine](/wiki/Wine "Wine"), and favored technique over brute strength in lightsaber combat.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Dooku was once a respected Jedi[[170]](#cite_note-Databank-170) and, during the Separatist Crisis, he was viewed as a "political idealist" by his former peers.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) During his time in the Order, Dooku chafed at the Jedi's disdain for technology.[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28) After meeting her, Dooku secretly kept in contact with his sister Jenza and grew close to her.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) His independent spirit helped push him away from the Jedi Order.[[171]](#cite_note-Jedi_vs_Sith-171) By the time he was a Sith, Dooku had come to believe the Jedi had wasted their powers but that he had not squandered his own.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67) Dooku became increasingly disillusioned with the Galactic Senate's corruption and the arrogance and apparent complacency of the Jedi Order, eventually coming to desire the downfall of both institutions he had once served.[[170]](#cite_note-Databank-170) Increasingly, Dooku became, in the words of his sister Jenza, corrupted as he gave into the dark side;[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) the man who once justified his actions as being in the name of overthrowing a corrupt Senate[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) became a corrupt leader himself,[[71]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-71) stealing from even his own people[[79]](#cite_note-Ruins_of_War-79)—those he had once protected[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)—and becoming obsessed with growing his own power. While he was beloved by the Separatist population[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) as a visionary and defender of democracy,[[163]](#cite_note-TM-C22:GfH-163) his true nature[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) was that of a Dark Lord of the Sith.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

After Sidious exploited Dooku's anger at the Republic to turn the count to the dark side,[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) Dooku—having become the Sith Lord Darth Tyranus—was a menacing, intelligent, powerful, manipulative, arrogant, and amoral, yet charismatic statesman with a refined and educated character befitting an aristocrat of the last years of the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era");[[170]](#cite_note-Databank-170)[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) in public, he maintained the image of a humanitarian leader who truly wanted what was best for the Confederacy, while in secret he looked for greater power as a Sith[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) and was willing to advance his plans with methods that included torture,[[106]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-106) assassination,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and even genocide.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) Because the Order served the Republic, Dooku believed the Jedi were dishonored and were not to be trusted.[[1]](#cite_note-SWEDooku-1) Dooku also protested the failure of the Republic, bringing numerous systems to the Confederacy, yet his true motives remained hidden. The Count truly wanted to rule a new Sith Empire at the side of Darth Sidious,[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28) whom he believed would bring order back to the galaxy.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67)

 [![Dooku obediently served Sidious while dreaming of taking his Master's place as the reigning Dark Lord of the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/LordSidiousCommands-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521030012) [![Dooku obediently served Sidious while dreaming of taking his Master's place as the reigning Dark Lord of the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/LordSidiousCommands-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130521030012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/LordSidiousCommands-Nightsisters.png/revision/latest?cb=20130521030012) 

Dooku obediently served Sidious while dreaming of taking his Master's place as the reigning Dark Lord of the Sith.

 

Despite her pleas for him to return to the light, Dooku was so committed to the dark side that he even had his own sister, Jenza, killed.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) Still, at least early in the war, Dooku's former master Yoda believed he could return Dooku to the light side if given the chance.[[172]](#cite_note-Sharing_the_Same_Face-172) Dooku was skilled at recruiting allies to his side, not only using his wealth, but also his natural charm and intense gravitas.[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) Nevertheless, he was willing to betray his own followers and allies, such as Asajj Ventress and Pre Vizsla,[[94]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-94) though he showed some regret over abandoning Ventress, angering his own master, Darth Sidious.[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74) He even betrayed and orchestrated the death of his former friend Sifo-Dyas. Dooku was very vindictive, as shown when he ordered devastating attacks against Mother Talzin and Hondo Ohnaka for crossing him in the past.[[8]](#cite_note-Massacre-8)[[118]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-118) Dooku was also quite fearless, and was willing to sacrifice himself in a final attempt to fully convert his last apprentice, Quinlan Vos, to the dark side by tempting Vos to strike him down after he mortally wounded Vos' lover, Ventress.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

Dooku initially felt remorse for betraying the Jedi and confronted Sidious in the wake of Qui-Gon Jinn's death. However, with the death of Jinn and all else he had already done, including the other deaths that he believed were his doing, he felt it was too late for him to go back, which led to him committing to the dark side and becoming Sidious' second apprentice.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) Further into his career as a Sith, despite his hatred toward the Jedi, he did still express fondness towards Qui-Gon. During his conversation with his Padawan's Padawan, Obi-Wan Kenobi, on Geonosis ten years after Qui-Gon's death, Dooku expressed some sadness over his Padawan's death.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) During a conversation via hologram concerning a [mission to Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia_(Kenobi_and_Skywalker) "Mission to Cato Neimoidia (Kenobi and Skywalker)"), in which Dooku was working to stonewall Kenobi's effort to clear the Republic's name in the [Cadesura disaster](/wiki/Cadesura_disaster "Cadesura disaster"), Kenobi invoked Jinn's name and asked the count if he had trusted his old apprentice, which Kenobi deemed to be a targeted counterattack to Dooku's own efforts. Reference to Jinn, indeed, created a minor but still present shift in Dooku's expression, which softened before Dooku could partially correct himself. Dooku responded that Jinn had been an honorable man and—when Kenobi pressed his attack, declaring he carried on the fallen master's teachings and, thus, was trustworthy—agreed to Kenobi's terms, albeit with two caveats of his own.[[173]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-173)

 [![The masterful lightsaber wielder Dooku](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Count_Dooku_Darth_Tyranus_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20190701053156) [![The masterful lightsaber wielder Dooku](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Count_Dooku_Darth_Tyranus_WotF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190701053156)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Count_Dooku_Darth_Tyranus_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20190701053156) 

The masterful lightsaber wielder Dooku

 

On Geonosis, Dooku also attempted to recruit Kenobi to his cause. The Separatist leader wished to persuade Kenobi to join him, and to that end, he revealed that the Republic was controlled by a Sith named Darth Sidious, although Kenobi refused to believe the duplicitous Dooku. Dooku was actually polite to Obi-Wan when he interrogated him as he did not act hostile in anyway. When Kenobi refused to join the treaty, Dooku had no problem with attempting to kill him.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) Dooku had intended for his claim on Geonosis to be too outrageous for Kenobi to believe, even though it was true, meaning he had fulfilled his plan.[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28) During the ensuing Clone Wars, Dooku would often tell Jedi he encountered that he was hunting the Sith Lord[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) he had told Kenobi of,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) yet the Jedi nevertheless saw that the Count used Sith powers.[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40) Indeed, the Jedi Order was aware of his true nature as a Sith Lord during the war.[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20)

While he was obedient to Sidious, he desired to eventually overthrow him and become the Sith master himself. Dooku was willing to betray Sidious for power; towards the end of the Clone Wars, he conspired with [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos")[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) and [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul")[[132]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-132) to attempt to overthrow Sidious. He had the same plans with Ventress[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) and Savage Opress.[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74) The Jedi Order taught that fear ultimately gave way to the dark side and, with it, suffering; Dooku fully admitted he had endured all the stages of the journey the Jedi had warned him of—fear, anger, hate, and suffering—during his path into the dark side. However, he insisted he had passed through that suffering and reached a state he defined as holding "ultimate power."[[20]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-20) Dooku also believed that the dark side was far more generous than the light.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67)

 [![In his final moments, Dooku realized he was a pawn to his master](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Betrayed.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210065749) [![In his final moments, Dooku realized he was a pawn to his master](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Betrayed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130210065749)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Betrayed.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210065749) 

In his final moments, Dooku realized he was a pawn to his master

 

However, he was unaware that he was just a pawn of Sidious, who was using him until it was time for Sidious to discard and replace him. He saw himself as Sidious' apprentice, but was unaware that Sidious never saw him that way and instead, viewed him as a pawn he could use until his purpose was served. While he desired to overthrow Sidious, he was unaware that Sidious similarly planned on having him replaced with Anakin. Dooku's obliviousness to his time running out and Sidious' true motives, led to his undoing. When Sidious instructed Anakin to kill a disarmed and beaten Dooku, Dooku was in a state of disbelief.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) At that point, Dooku gained some new understandings of what had transpired;[[170]](#cite_note-Databank-170) he had been used and was now being betrayed by his own secret master, and that betrayal was the Sith way.[[174]](#cite_note-Databank_BG-174)

## Powers and abilities[]

:   "*Powerful you have become, Dooku. The dark side I sense in you.*"  
    "*I have become more powerful than any Jedi. Even you.*"
:   ―Yoda and Count Dooku[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![Dooku was a powerful Force wielder and a master lightsaber duelist.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/CountDooku-SWL-2025UnitCardUpdate.png/revision/latest?cb=20250624190049) [![Dooku was a powerful Force wielder and a master lightsaber duelist.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/CountDooku-SWL-2025UnitCardUpdate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250624190049)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/CountDooku-SWL-2025UnitCardUpdate.png/revision/latest?cb=20250624190049) 

Dooku was a powerful Force wielder and a master lightsaber duelist.

 

A man of formidable power that was exemplified by his Sith name of Tyranus,[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67) Dooku was a highly skillful lightsaber duelist even in his old age. During his time as a Jedi, he was known as one of the Order's finest swordsmen; it was said that Yoda was his only superior and Mace Windu was his only equal. On Geonosis, Dooku was able to easily defeat both Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker one immediately after the other, and then go on to fight Yoda himself. Dooku was able to contend with Yoda but elected to retreat when he was unable to defeat his former master.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) He would often prove to be equal and even superior to Skywalker and Kenobi even as their skill grew during the Clone Wars,[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) dueling Skywalker on several occasions, proving to be his superior[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67) until Skywalker was powerful enough to overcome the Count.[[175]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_Undercover-175)

Among the most skilled swordsmen [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") had ever seen, Dooku was a practitioner of the second form of lightsaber combat, [Makashi](/wiki/Form_II "Form II"). Makashi was designed specifically for lightsaber-to-lightsaber duels.[[176]](#cite_note-KoF-176)

 [![Dooku wielded a curved-hilt lightsaber and favored the second form of lightsaber combat.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/CountDookuGeonosis-SWBC61.png/revision/latest?cb=20240218045332) [![Dooku wielded a curved-hilt lightsaber and favored the second form of lightsaber combat.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/CountDookuGeonosis-SWBC61.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240218045332)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/CountDookuGeonosis-SWBC61.png/revision/latest?cb=20240218045332) 

Dooku wielded a curved-hilt lightsaber and favored the second form of lightsaber combat.

 

In addition to his formidable lightsaber skills, Dooku was very knowledgeable and skilled in the use of the Force. He demonstrated great prowess and strength in the use of telekinesis. During his duels with Ventress and his escape from Hondo's pirates, he displayed great skill at using telekinesis in finer, more precise tasks, such as disarming Ventress while also levitating her against a wall during her failed attempt to kill him with Savage Opress. He was even capable of telekinetically manipulating people's motor skills, such as when he [Force choked](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") while simultaneously forcing [Turk Falso](/wiki/Turk_Falso "Turk Falso") to take out his blaster and shoot his comrade, while he performed a similar feat when he made Padmé Amidala aim at and shoot [Bec Lawise](/wiki/Bec_Lawise "Bec Lawise").[[88]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-88)[[97]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-97)

Dooku was also highly skilled in the use of Force lightning, using it as both a means of torture and execution, and was able to use it in conjunction with telekinesis, usually to send a person flying with his lightning or even to levitate his opponents while using his lightning on them, as he demonstrated on Ventress and two Nightsister assassins.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)[[74]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-74)

## Equipment[]

:   "*That lightsaber. It's—Where did you get that?*"  
    "*I made it, of course.*"
:   ―[Jak'zin](/wiki/Jak%27zin "Jak'zin") and Dooku, on Dooku's lightsaber[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29)

 [![Dooku was presented a Sith Infiltrator for his use after becoming a Sith apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/CountDookuSithInfiltrator-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20220716003619) [![Dooku was presented a Sith Infiltrator for his use after becoming a Sith apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/CountDookuSithInfiltrator-SWZ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220716003619)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/CountDookuSithInfiltrator-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20220716003619) 

Dooku was presented a Sith Infiltrator for his use after becoming a Sith apprentice.

 

Conscious of his aristocratic status, Dooku preferred to wear elegant garments—whether as a member of the Jedi Order, the Count of his homeworld Serenno, or as the Sith Lord Darth Tyranus—befitting his elevated station.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67) His wardrobe included a hand-woven tunic made on [Vjun](/wiki/Vjun "Vjun") and brown [Serennian cloaks](/wiki/Serennian_cloak "Serennian cloak"), that were an emblem of the Count of Serenno, held by a clasp of [Serenno silver](/wiki/Serenno_silver "Serenno silver").[[177]](#cite_note-VE-177) He variously wore similar cloaks with[[24]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-24) and without a built-in hood.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) In addition, his sleepwear consisted of dark blue exquisite pajamas that he purchased from one of the most exclusive tailors in the galaxy. Dooku's pajamas were stitched from the finest [silks](/wiki/Silk "Silk"), its elegant patterning rivaled only by the prominent monogram on his front chest pocket.[[67]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-67)

 [![Dooku's preferred ship during the Clone Wars was a Punworcca 116-class solar sailer.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/SolarSailer-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250207064147) [![Dooku's preferred ship during the Clone Wars was a Punworcca 116-class solar sailer.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/SolarSailer-CGSWG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250207064147)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/SolarSailer-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250207064147) 

Dooku's preferred ship during the Clone Wars was a Punworcca 116-class solar sailer.

 

In addition to the various capital ships he made use of as leader of the Confederacy of Independent Systems, Dooku also owned several personal vehicles. After becoming apprentice to Darth Sidious, he was presented with his own [Sith Infiltrator](/wiki/Scimitar "Scimitar").[[75]](#cite_note-Sith_Infiltrator-75) During the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), the Geonosians gifted Dooku with a [personal](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_solar_sailer "Count Dooku's solar sailer") [*Punworcca 116*-class](/wiki/Punworcca_116-class_interstellar_sloop "Punworcca 116-class interstellar sloop") [solar sailer](/wiki/Solar_sailer "Solar sailer") and [Flitknot Speeder Bike](/wiki/Flitknot_Speeder_Bike "Flitknot Speeder Bike"), both of which he used to escape the Battle of Geonosis[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) and throughout the ensuing Clone Wars.[[80]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-80)

## Behind the scenes[]

### Portrayal[]

:   "*He's very aloof, very self-contained, obviously completely fearless. He is extremely intelligent, perhaps more so than almost anyone else. He's obviously a man of immense power. I don't suppose that the question of moral values entered into his head. He's not immoral—he's amoral. Morality is a word that doesn't figure in his vocabulary at all. It's power. Which is something that exists very much in our world today.*"
:   ―Sir Christopher Lee's thoughts on his character Dooku[[178]](#cite_note-Homing_Beacon-178)

 [![Christopher Lee with George Lucas on the set of Attack of the Clones](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Lee_Lucas_EP2_BTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20160407222206) [![Christopher Lee with George Lucas on the set of Attack of the Clones](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Lee_Lucas_EP2_BTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20160407222206)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Lee_Lucas_EP2_BTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20160407222206) 

Christopher Lee with George Lucas on the set of *Attack of the Clones*

 

Dooku was portrayed by the late Sir [Christopher Lee](/wiki/Christopher_Lee "Christopher Lee") in [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") and [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"). [Kyle Rowling](/wiki/Kyle_Rowling "Kyle Rowling") portrayed Dooku during most of the character's lightsaber sequences, due to Lee's inability to enact these physical scenes because of his age. Rowling's head was digitally replaced with Lee's during post-production.[[179]](#cite_note-Episode_II_Cast_and_Crew-179)

 [![Early concept art of Dooku by Iain McCaig](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/EarlyDookuConceptIainMcCaig-SWBC61.png/revision/latest?cb=20240218051123) [![Early concept art of Dooku by Iain McCaig](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/EarlyDookuConceptIainMcCaig-SWBC61.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240218051123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/EarlyDookuConceptIainMcCaig-SWBC61.png/revision/latest?cb=20240218051123) 

Early concept art of Dooku by Iain McCaig

 

Dooku's character underwent multiple development iterations during the creative process of *Attack of the Clones*; artists [Iain McCaig](/wiki/Iain_McCaig "Iain McCaig") and [Dermot Power](/wiki/Dermot_Power "Dermot Power") experimented with various female Sith designs, including dark queens, robotic warriors, and vampiric witches as well as a shapeshifting alien concept that eventually evolved into [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell"), until [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") eventually decided on the idea of a battle scarred Jedi warrior who parted ways with the Jedi Order. The final designs of the character were intended to reflect the menacing atmosphere conveyed by [Peter Cushing](/wiki/Peter_Cushing "Peter Cushing")'s portrayal of [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") Wilhuff Tarkin in [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope").[[180]](#cite_note-old-db-bts-180)

Christopher Lee reprised his role in the [*Star Wars: The Clone Wars* film](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(film) "Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)"), while [Corey Burton](/wiki/Corey_Burton "Corey Burton") would voice Dooku in the [subsequent TV series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") and the animated anthology series [*Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)").

### Character origins and name[]

:   "*Don't think of it as a first name, but a singular name. The aristocracy of Serenno only use one name, but use the format Dooku of House Serenno, not Dooku Serenno.*"
:   ―Cavan Scott on whether "Dooku" is the character's first or last name[[181]](#cite_note-Cavan_Scott_Dooku_name_tweet_1-181)

 [![The audio drama Dooku: Jedi Lost covered the backstory of Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/DookuJediLost-V1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190330214347) [![The audio drama Dooku: Jedi Lost covered the backstory of Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/DookuJediLost-V1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190330214347)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/DookuJediLost-V1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190330214347) 

The audio drama *Dooku: Jedi Lost* covered the backstory of Count Dooku.

 

The name "Dooku" was based on the [Japanese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language "wikipedia:Japanese language") word "doku," meaning poison.[[182]](#cite_note-Lord_of_Misrule:_The_Autobiography_of_Christopher_Lee-182) In the [Galician](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician_language "wikipedia:Galician language") and [Portuguese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language "wikipedia:Portuguese language") languages, "do cu," pronounced exactly as in "Dooku," means "from the ass" or "of the ass." For this reason, Dooku's name was changed to "Dookan" in [Brazil](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brazil "wikipedia:Brazil") and [Portugal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portugal).[[183]](#cite_note-Globo-183)

*Tyranus*—or more properly, *Tyrannos*—is an ancient [Greek](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language "wikipedia:Greek language") word, originally used to describe someone who ruled a city-state after overthrowing the preexisting government. It was a legitimate form of government and the word's meaning was not unfavorable in itself, but over time, as democracy developed, it gained negative connotations and came to mean "oppressor" or "tyrant."[[184]](#cite_note-Tyrant-184)

When developing the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") audio drama *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")*,[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) author [Cavan Scott](/wiki/Cavan_Scott "Cavan Scott") considered giving the count another name but ultimately decided against it. As such,[[185]](#cite_note-Cavan_Scott_Dooku_name_tweet_2-185) Scott further noted Serennian aristocracy only use a singular name while being formally addressed as members of House Serenno. In effect, Dooku's full name is not "Dooku Serenno," with "Dooku" instead being a singular name, but the count would answer to the formal title "Dooku of House Serenno."[[181]](#cite_note-Cavan_Scott_Dooku_name_tweet_1-181)

### Discrepancies[]

According to one *[Star Wars: Card Trader](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Card_Trader "Star Wars: Card Trader")*, San Hill - Banking Clan Chairman - *Base Series 1*, Dooku allied with Poggle the Lesser and San Hill in a plot to destroy their unstable ally Grievous and transform him into a cyborg to serve them.[[186]](#cite_note-Base_Series_1-186) [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo") of the [Lucasfilm Story Group](/wiki/Lucasfilm_Story_Group "Lucasfilm Story Group") said this was to be disregarded as an outdated reference to Grievous's backstory in *Star Wars* Legends.[[187]](#cite_note-Lost_Pablo_Tweet-187) However, other canon sources have brought in details of Grievous's Legends backstory, including Dooku's role in the shuttle crash that injured Grievous.[[50]](#cite_note-HC_8-50)

 [![Dooku reflects on the ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/BattleOfNaboo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20221023125850) [![Dooku reflects on the ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/BattleOfNaboo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221023125850)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/BattleOfNaboo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20221023125850) 

Dooku reflects on the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo")

 

During a question session for [*The Clone Wars*: The Lost Missions](/wiki/The_Clone_Wars:_The_Lost_Missions "The Clone Wars: The Lost Missions"), [Dave Filoni](/wiki/Dave_Filoni "Dave Filoni") revealed that Darth Sidious had Dooku and Maul as Sith apprentices concurrently.[[42]](#cite_note-TCW_Lost_Missions_Q&A-42) However, the fifth slide of Sidious' [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") biography gallery says that the Sith Lord brought Dooku into the Sith Order sometime after becoming Supreme Chancellor of the Republic. This slide is placed after[[188]](#cite_note-Sidious_BioGal5-188) those which cover the events of [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"),[[189]](#cite_note-Sidious_BioGal_2,_3,_and_4-189) the film in which Maul was thought to be killed.[[66]](#cite_note-Episode_I-66) *[Star Wars: Secrets of the Sith](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Secrets_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Secrets of the Sith")* stated that Dooku became a Sith apprentice after Maul's supposed death.[[41]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-41) Nonetheless, *The Clone Wars* episode "[The Lost One](/wiki/The_Lost_One "The Lost One")" established Dooku needed to have some association with the Sith before *The Phantom Menace*, given he killed Sifo-Dyas during the chancellery of Finis Valorum,[[45]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-45) who was deposed in that film.[[66]](#cite_note-Episode_I-66) [*Age of Republic - Count Dooku* 1](/wiki/Age_of_Republic_-_Count_Dooku_1 "Age of Republic - Count Dooku 1"), *[Master & Apprentice](/wiki/Master_%26_Apprentice "Master & Apprentice")*, and *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* all establish that Dooku left the Jedi before Qui-Gon Jinn's death.[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29)[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) However, the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") [Fantasy Flight Games](/wiki/Fantasy_Flight_Games "Fantasy Flight Games") sourcebook *[Rise of the Separatists](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Separatists "Rise of the Separatists")* states that Dooku credited Jinn's death as his reason for leaving the Order.[[40]](#cite_note-Rise-40)

The [*Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)") episode "[The Sith Lord](/wiki/The_Sith_Lord "The Sith Lord")" later affirmed that Dooku was working alongside Darth Sidious during the events of *The Phantom Menace*, but he was aware of Maul being Sidious' apprentice, had not fully committed himself to the dark side, and did not yet have his [Sith lightsaber](/wiki/Sith_lightsaber "Sith lightsaber"). Upon the death of Yaddle in the episode, Dooku formally became Sidious' pupil,[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) thereby mending the contradicting sources; Dooku was indeed partnered with Sidious and aided in the Sith Lord's efforts, but he was not the Sith apprentice Darth Tyranus until Maul's supposed demise.

 [![Dooku (left) depicted with gray hair during his time as a Jedi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DookuYodaYounglings-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190215021255) [![Dooku (left) depicted with gray hair during his time as a Jedi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DookuYodaYounglings-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20190215021255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DookuYodaYounglings-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190215021255) 

Dooku (left) depicted with gray hair during his time as a Jedi

 

There is an additional discrepancy for Dooku's aging; flashbacks in *Age of Republic - Count Dooku* 1 feature Dooku with white hair while still in the Jedi Order.[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29) while in Dooku: Jedi Lost, an apparition of Jedi Ky Narec appearing to Asajj Ventress explicitly describes Dooku's beard as having turned to gray during the time the two men knew each other as part of the Order.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) "The Sith Lord" later featured Dooku after leaving the Order, however he is visibly younger in this appearance, instead having black hair.[[21]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-21) As the flashbacks in the *Age of Republic* comic are framed as the memories of Jak'zin,[[29]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku_1-29) this article assumes the character simply misremembered Dooku's appearance over the years.

Most stories[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36)[[123]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-123) and sources[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28)[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39)[[169]](#cite_note-RiseFall-169)[[190]](#cite_note-HC15DB-190) either suggest[[36]](#cite_note-Tarkin-36)[[28]](#cite_note-CVD-28)[[169]](#cite_note-RiseFall-169) or outright affirm[[123]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-123)[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39) that Dooku knew the Separatist Alliance was destinated to lose the Clone Wars while the Galactic Republic would be transformed into the new Sith Empire.[[39]](#cite_note-BC61-39) However, the [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025") novel *[Master of Evil](/wiki/Master_of_Evil "Master of Evil")* features an internal monologue from Dooku in which the count reflects that it is the Separatists who will win the war so as to usher in his and Sidious's new Sith regime.[[191]](#cite_note-Master_of_Evil-191) This article sides with the majority of sources and disregards this sentence.

### Non-canon history[]

 [![Dooku in The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/DookuTrainingManual.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221022132813) [![Dooku in The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/DookuTrainingManual.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20221022132813)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/DookuTrainingManual.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221022132813) 

Dooku in *The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual*

 

:   "*As a Sith Lord, Dooku was great at swordplay, strategy, and kneeling before dudes in hooded capes.*"
