:   ―*The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual*[[192]](#cite_note-Training_Manual-192)

Dooku is mentioned in the [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") non-[canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") reference book *[LEGO Star Wars: The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Official_Stormtrooper_Training_Manual "LEGO Star Wars: The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual")*, which is written as an in-universe [guidebook](/wiki/The_Official_Stormtrooper_Training_Manual "The Official Stormtrooper Training Manual") for [stormtrooper](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") [cadets](/wiki/Cadet "Cadet"). It established that Dooku was a famous historical figure, used his curved lightsaber to cut the crusts off [sandwiches](/wiki/Sandwich "Sandwich"), and went by the rap name **MC Eyebrows**. It also explained that he scowled so much due to him surgically removing his other facial expressions, and among his defining attributes was kneeling before robed individuals.[[192]](#cite_note-Training_Manual-192)

[↑](#cite_ref-Yoda_4_22-0) [*Yoda* 4](/wiki/Yoda_4 "Yoda 4") 23. [↑](#cite_ref-86_BBY_23-0) The [script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)") of *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* states that Dooku was sixteen years old during his [Initiate Trials](/wiki/Initiate_Trials "Initiate Trials"), thereby placing the trials and their immediate aftermath to around [86 BBY](/wiki/86_BBY "86 BBY"), as *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates his birth to [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY"). 24. ↑ [24.0](#cite_ref-Sacrifice_24-0) [24.1](#cite_ref-Sacrifice_24-1) [24.2](#cite_ref-Sacrifice_24-2) [24.3](#cite_ref-Sacrifice_24-3) [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[Sacrifice](/wiki/Sacrifice_(episode) "Sacrifice (episode)")" 25. [↑](#cite_ref-85_BBY_date_25-0) The [script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)") of *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* establishes that Dooku was seventeen [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") old during the [Protobranch solar storm](/wiki/Protobranch_solar_storm "Protobranch solar storm"). Thus, the solar storm must have occurred around 85 BBY, as *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates his birth to [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY"). 26. [↑](#cite_ref-82_BBY_26-0) The [script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)") of *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* states that Dooku is twenty years old during the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Countess_Anya "Funeral of Countess Anya") of Countess [Anya](/wiki/Anya_(Serenno) "Anya (Serenno)"), meaning that the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral "Funeral") must have occurred around [82 BBY](/wiki/82_BBY "82 BBY"), as *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates his birth to [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY"). 27. [↑](#cite_ref-33_BBY_note_47-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of [*Darth Maul* (2017) 3](/wiki/Darth_Maul_(2017)_3 "Darth Maul (2017) 3")—which features [IG-100 MagnaGuards](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard")—to [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY"). "[The Separatists](/wiki/The_Separatists_(reference_book) "The Separatists (reference book)")" establishes that [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") requested the creation of an advanced [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid")—which became the IG-100 upon **Dooku** putting in the order for their creation—after joining the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), which Grievous joined after a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") intervention into the [Kaleesh-Yam'rii war](/wiki/Kaleesh-Yam%27rii_war "Kaleesh-Yam'rii war"). As the IG-100 must exist by 33 BBY, that intervention must have happened by that [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"). 48. The aristocracy of Serenno only use one name, but use the format Dooku of House Serenno, not Dooku Serenno. In my mind it started as a sign of the importance of independence which runs through Serenno culture."
